bytes into Event types\n+// Handles ANSI escape sequences for keys, mouse, and special characters\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const event_mod = @import(\"event.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Event = event_mod.Event;\n+pub const Key = event_mod.Key;\n+pub const KeyCode = event_mod.KeyCode;\n+pub const Modifiers = event_mod.Modifiers;\n+pub const Mouse = event_mod.Mouse;\n+pub const MouseKind = event_mod.MouseKind;\n+pub const Size = event_mod.Size;\n+\n+/// Input parser state machine.\n+/// Parses raw terminal input bytes into Event types.\n+pub const Input = struct {\n+    /// Buffer for incomplete escape sequences\n+    buffer: [32]u8 = undefined,\n+    /// Number of bytes in buffer\n+    buffer_len: usize = 0,\n+    /// Whether we're in a paste sequence\n+    in_paste: bool = false,\n+\n+    const Self = @This();\n+\n+    /// Initialize a new input parser.\n+    pub fn init() Self {\n+        return .{};\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse input bytes and return an event if one is complete.\n+    /// May consume partial input for multi-byte sequences.\n+    pub fn parse(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n+        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n+            return null;\n+        }\n+\n+        // Handle bracketed paste mode\n+        if (self.in_paste) {\n+            return self.parsePaste(bytes);\n+        }\n+\n+        // Check for escape sequence\n+        if (bytes[0] == 0x1b) {\n+            return self.parseEscape(bytes);\n+        }\n+\n+        // Handle control characters\n+        if (bytes[0] < 0x20) {\n+            return self.parseControl(bytes[0]);\n+        }\n+\n+        // Handle regular UTF-8 character\n+        return self.parseUtf8(bytes);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse a control character (0x00-0x1F).\n+    fn parseControl(self: *Self, byte: u8) ?Event {\n+        _ = self;\n+        return switch (byte) {\n+            0x00 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = ' ' }, .modifiers = .{ .ctrl = true } } }, // Ctrl+Space\n+            0x09 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .tab } }, // Tab\n+            0x0a, 0x0d => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .enter } }, // Enter (LF or CR)\n+            0x7f => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .backspace } }, // Backspace (DEL)\n+            // Ctrl+A through Ctrl+Z (excluding tab=0x09, enter=0x0a, and 0x0d)\n+            0x01...0x08, 0x0b, 0x0c, 0x0e...0x1a => |b| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = 'a' + (b - 1) }, .modifiers = .{ .ctrl = true } } },\n+            0x1b => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } }, // Escape (handled elsewhere)\n+            else => null,\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse an escape sequence.\n+    fn parseEscape(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n+        if (bytes.len == 1) {\n+            // Just ESC by itself\n+            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n+        }\n+\n+        const second = bytes[1];\n+\n+        // CSI sequence (ESC [)\n+        if (second == '[') {\n+            return self.parseCsi(bytes[2..]);\n+        }\n+\n+        // SS3 sequence (ESC O)\n+        if (second == 'O') {\n+            return self.parseSs3(bytes[2..]);\n+        }\n+\n+        // Alt+Escape\n+        if (second == 0x1b) {\n+            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape, .modifiers = .{ .alt = true } } };\n+        }\n+\n+        // Alt+key (printable ASCII)\n+        if (second >= 0x20 and second < 0x7f) {\n+            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = second }, .modifiers = .{ .alt = true } } };\n+        }\n+\n+        return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse a CSI (Control Sequence Introducer) sequence.\n+    /// Format: ESC [ <params> <final>\n+    fn parseCsi(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n+        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n+            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n+        }\n+\n+        // Check for mouse sequences\n+        if (bytes[0] == 'M' or bytes[0] == '<') {\n+            return self.parseMouse(bytes);\n+        }\n+\n+        // Check for bracketed paste\n+        if (bytes.len >= 4 and bytes[0] == '2' and bytes[1] == '0' and bytes[2] == '0' and bytes[3] == '~') {\n+            self.in_paste = true;\n+            return null;\n+        }\n+\n+        // Parse arrow keys and simple sequences\n+        if (bytes.len >= 1) {\n+            return switch (bytes[0]) {\n+                'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up } },\n+                'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down } },\n+                'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right } },\n+                'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left } },\n+                'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home } },\n+                'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end } },\n+                'Z' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .backtab } }, // Shift+Tab\n+                else => self.parseCsiParams(bytes),\n+            };\n+        }\n+\n+        return null;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse CSI sequences with parameters.\n+    fn parseCsiParams(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n+        _ = self;\n+\n+        // Find the final character\n+        var i: usize = 0;\n+        var param1: u16 = 0;\n+        var param2: u16 = 0;\n+        var in_second_param = false;\n+\n+        while (i < bytes.len) : (i += 1) {\n+            const c = bytes[i];\n+            if (c >= '0' and c <= '9') {\n+                if (in_second_param) {\n+                    param2 = param2 * 10 + (c - '0');\n+                } else {\n+                    param1 = param1 * 10 + (c - '0');\n+                }\n+            } else if (c == ';') {\n+                in_second_param = true;\n+            } else {\n+                // Final character\n+                return parseCsiFinal(c, param1, param2);\n+            }\n+        }\n+\n+        return null;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse the final character of a CSI sequence.\n+    fn parseCsiFinal(final: u8, param1: u16, param2: u16) ?Event {\n+        // Extract modifiers from param2 (CSI 1;2A = Shift+Up, etc.)\n+        const mods = modifiersFromParam(param2);\n+\n+        return switch (final) {\n+            'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up, .modifiers = mods } },\n+            'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down, .modifiers = mods } },\n+            'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right, .modifiers = mods } },\n+            'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left, .modifiers = mods } },\n+            'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n+            'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n+            '~' => switch (param1) {\n+                1 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n+                2 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .insert, .modifiers = mods } },\n+                3 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .delete, .modifiers = mods } },\n+                4 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n+                5 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .page_up, .modifiers = mods } },\n+                6 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .page_down, .modifiers = mods } },\n+                7 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n+                8 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n+                11...15 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 10) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F1-F5\n+                17...21 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 11) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F6-F10\n+                23, 24 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 12) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F11-F12\n+                200 => null, // Bracketed paste start (handled elsewhere)\n+                201 => null, // Bracketed paste end (handled elsewhere)\n+                else => null,\n+            },\n+            'P' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 1 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F1\n+            'Q' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 2 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F2\n+            'R' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 3 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F3\n+            'S' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 4 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F4\n+            else => null,\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Convert modifier parameter to Modifiers struct.\n+    /// Terminal convention: 1=none, 2=shift, 3=alt, 4=shift+alt, 5=ctrl, etc.\n+    fn modifiersFromParam(param: u16) Modifiers {\n+        if (param == 0 or param == 1) {\n+            return Modifiers{};\n+        }\n+\n+        const p = param - 1;\n+        return Modifiers{\n+            .shift = (p & 1) != 0,\n+            .alt = (p & 2) != 0,\n+            .ctrl = (p & 4) != 0,\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse an SS3 (Single Shift 3) sequence.\n+    /// Used by some terminals for function keys and keypad.\n+    fn parseSs3(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n+        _ = self;\n+        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n+            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n+        }\n+\n+        return switch (bytes[0]) {\n+            'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up } },\n+            'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down } },\n+            'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right } },\n+            'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left } },\n+            'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home } },\n+            'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end } },\n+            'P' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 1 } } },\n+            'Q' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 2 } } },\n+            'R' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 3 } } },\n+            'S' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 4 } } },\n+            else => null,\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse mouse sequences (X10 or SGR mode).\n+    fn parseMouse(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n+        _ = self;\n+\n+        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n+            return null;\n+        }\n+\n+        // SGR mode: ESC [ < Cb ; Cx ; Cy M/m\n+        if (bytes[0] == '<') {\n+            return parseMouseSgr(bytes[1..]);\n+        }\n+\n+        // X10 mode: ESC [ M Cb Cx Cy\n+        if (bytes[0] == 'M') {\n+            return parseMouseX10(bytes[1..]);\n+        }\n+\n+        return null;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse SGR mouse sequence.\n+    /// Format: <Cb;Cx;Cy M or <Cb;Cx;Cy m\n+    fn parseMouseSgr(bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n+        var i: usize = 0;\n+        var cb: u16 = 0;\n+        var cx: u16 = 0;\n+        var cy: u16 = 0;\n+        var param_index: u8 = 0;\n+\n+        while (i < bytes.len) : (i += 1) {\n+            const c = bytes[i];\n+            if (c >= '0' and c <= '9') {\n+                switch (param_index) {\n+                    0 => cb = cb * 10 + (c - '0'),\n+                    1 => cx = cx * 10 + (c - '0'),\n+                    2 => cy = cy * 10 + (c - '0'),\n+                    else => {},\n+                }\n+            } else if (c == ';') {\n+                param_index += 1;\n+            } else if (c == 'M' or c == 'm') {\n+                // M = button press, m = button release\n+                const is_release = (c == 'm');\n+\n+                // Decode button and modifiers from cb\n+                const button = @as(u8, @intCast(cb & 0x03));\n+                const shift = (cb & 0x04) != 0;\n+                const alt = (cb & 0x08) != 0;\n+                const ctrl = (cb & 0x10) != 0;\n+                const motion = (cb & 0x20) != 0;\n+                const wheel = (cb & 0x40) != 0;\n+\n+                const kind: MouseKind = if (wheel)\n+                    if (button == 0) .scroll_up else .scroll_down\n+                else if (motion)\n+                    .drag\n+                else if (is_release)\n+                    .up\n+                else\n+                    .down;\n+\n+                // SGR coordinates are 1-based\n+                const x = if (cx > 0) cx - 1 else 0;\n+                const y = if (cy > 0) cy - 1 else 0;\n+\n+                return Event{\n+                    .mouse = .{\n+                        .x = x,\n+                        .y = y,\n+                        .kind = kind,\n+                        .modifiers = .{\n+                            .shift = shift,\n+                            .alt = alt,\n+                            .ctrl = ctrl,\n+                        },\n+                    },\n+                };\n+            }\n+        }\n+\n+        return null;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse X10 mouse sequence.\n+    /// Format: M Cb Cx Cy (all encoded as Cb+32, Cx+32, Cy+32)\n+    fn parseMouseX10(bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n+        if (bytes.len < 3) {\n+            return null;\n+        }\n+\n+        const cb = bytes[0] -| 32;\n+        const cx = bytes[1] -| 32;\n+        const cy = bytes[2] -| 32;\n+\n+        const button = cb & 0x03;\n+        const shift = (cb & 0x04) != 0;\n+        const alt = (cb & 0x08) != 0;\n+        const ctrl = (cb & 0x10) != 0;\n+        const motion = (cb & 0x20) != 0;\n+        const wheel = (cb & 0x40) != 0;\n+\n+        const kind: MouseKind = if (wheel)\n+            if (button == 0) .scroll_up else .scroll_down\n+        else if (motion)\n+            .drag\n+        else if (button == 3)\n+            .up // X10 uses button 3 for release\n+        else\n+            .down;\n+\n+        return Event{\n+            .mouse = .{\n+                .x = cx,\n+                .y = cy,\n+                .kind = kind,\n+                .modifiers = .{\n+                    .shift = shift,\n+                    .alt = alt,\n+                    .ctrl = ctrl,\n+                },\n+            },\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse a paste sequence.\n+    fn parsePaste(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n+        // Look for paste end sequence: ESC [ 2 0 1 ~\n+        const end_seq = \"\\x1b[201~\";\n+        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, bytes, end_seq)) |_| {\n+            self.in_paste = false;\n+            // For now, we don't expose paste content as events\n+            // Future: could return a paste event with content\n+        }\n+        return null;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Parse a UTF-8 character sequence.\n+    fn parseUtf8(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n+        _ = self;\n+\n+        // Determine UTF-8 sequence length from first byte\n+        const len = utf8ByteLen(bytes[0]);\n+\n+        if (len == 0) {\n+            return null;\n+        }\n+\n+        if (bytes.len < len) {\n+            // Incomplete sequence\n+            return null;\n+        }\n+\n+        // Decode the codepoint\n+        const codepoint = std.unicode.utf8Decode(bytes[0..len]) catch {\n+            return null;\n+        };\n+\n+        return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = codepoint } } };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Get the length of a UTF-8 sequence from its first byte.\n+fn utf8ByteLen(byte: u8) usize {\n+    if (byte < 0x80) return 1;\n+    if (byte < 0xc0) return 0; // Continuation byte\n+    if (byte < 0xe0) return 2;\n+    if (byte < 0xf0) return 3;\n+    if (byte < 0xf8) return 4;\n+    return 0;\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic input parsing\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: Input.init creates parser\" {\n+    const input = Input.init();\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), input.buffer_len);\n+    try std.testing.expect(!input.in_paste);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: parse single ASCII character\" {\n+    var input = Input.init();\n+    const event = input.parse(\"a\");\n+  21    /// Number of bytes in buffer\n    22    buffer_len: usize = 0,\n    23    /// Whether we're in a paste sequence\n    24    in_paste: bool = false,\n    25\n    26    const Self = @This();\n    27\n    28    /// Initialize a new input parser.\n    29    pub fn init() Self {\n    30        return .{};\n    31    }\n    32\n    33    /// Parse input bytes and return an event if one is complete.\n    34    /// May consume partial input for multi-byte sequences.\n    35    pub fn parse(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n    36        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n    37            return null;\n    38        }\n    39\n    40        // Handle bracketed paste mode\n    41        if (self.in_paste) {\n    42            return self.parsePaste(bytes);\n    43        }\n    44\n    45        // Check for escape sequence\n    46        if (bytes[0] == 0x1b) {\n    47            return self.parseEscape(bytes);\n    48        }\n    49\n    50        // Handle control characters\n    51        if (bytes[0] < 0x20) {\n    52            return self.parseControl(bytes[0]);\n    53        }\n    54\n    55        // Handle regular UTF-8 character\n    56        return self.parseUtf8(bytes);\n    57    }\n    58\n    59    /// Parse a control character (0x00-0x1F).\n    60    fn parseControl(self: *Self, byte: u8) ?Event {\n    61        _ = self;\n    62        return switch (byte) {\n    63            0x00 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = ' ' }, .modifiers = .{ .ctrl = true } } }, // Ctrl+Space\n    64            0x09 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .tab } }, // Tab\n    65            0x0a, 0x0d => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .enter } }, // Enter (LF or CR)\n    66            0x7f => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .backspace } }, // Backspace (DEL)\n    67            // Ctrl+A through Ctrl+Z (excluding tab=0x09, enter=0x0a, and 0x0d)\n    68            0x01...0x08, 0x0b, 0x0c, 0x0e...0x1a => |b| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = 'a' + (b - 1) }, .modifiers = .{ .ctrl = true } } },\n    69            0x1b => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } }, // Escape (handled elsewhere)\n    70            else => null,\n    71        };\n    72    }\n    73\n    74    /// Parse an escape sequence.\n    75    fn parseEscape(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n    76        if (bytes.len == 1) {\n    77            // Just ESC by itself\n    78            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n    79        }\n    80\n    81        const second = bytes[1];\n    82\n    83        // CSI sequence (ESC [)\n    84        if (second == '[') {\n    85            return self.parseCsi(bytes[2..]);\n    86        }\n    87\n    88        // SS3 sequence (ESC O)\n    89        if (second == 'O') {\n    90            return self.parseSs3(bytes[2..]);\n    91        }\n    92\n    93        // Alt+Escape\n    94        if (second == 0x1b) {\n    95            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape, .modifiers = .{ .alt = Introducer) sequence.\n   107    /// Format: ESC [ <params> <final>\n   108    fn parseCsi(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n   109        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n   110            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n   111        }\n   112\n   113        // Check for mouse sequences\n   114        if (bytes[0] == 'M' or bytes[0] == '<') {\n   115            return self.parseMouse(bytes);\n   116        }\n   117\n   118        // Check for bracketed paste\n   119        if (bytes.len >= 4 and bytes[0] == '2' and bytes[1] == '0' and bytes[2] == '0' and bytes[3] == '~') {\n   120            self.in_paste = true;\n   121            return null;\n   122        }\n   123\n   124        // Parse arrow keys and simple sequences\n   125        if (bytes.len >= 1) {\n   126            return switch (bytes[0]) {\n   127                'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up } },\n   128                'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down } },\n   129                'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right } },\n   130                'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left } },\n   131                'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home } },\n   132                'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end } },\n   133                'Z' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .backtab } }, // Shift+Tab\n   134                else => self.parseCsiParams(bytes),\n   135            };\n   136        }\n   137\n   138        return null;\n   139    }\n   140\n   141    /// Parse CSI sequences with parameters.\n   142    fn parseCsiParams(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n   143        _ = self;\n   144\n   145        // Find the final character\n   146        var i: usize = 0;\n   147        var param1: u16 = 0;\n   148        var param2: u16 = 0;\n   149        var in_second_param = false;\n   150\n   151        while (i < bytes.len) : (i += 1) {\n   152            const c = bytes[i];\n   153            if (c >= '0' and c <= '9') {\n   154                if (in_second_param) {\n   155                    param2 = param2 * 10 + (c - '0');\n   156                } else {\n   157                    param1 = param1 * 10 + (c - '0');\n   158                }\n   159            } else if (c == ';') {\n   160                in_second_param = true;\n   161            } else {\n   162                // Final character\n   163                return parseCsiFinal(c, param1, param2);\n   164            }\n   165        }\n   166\n   167        return null;\n   168    }\n   169\n   170    /// Parse the final character of a CSI sequence.\n   171    fn parseCsiFinal(final: u8, param1: u16, param2: u16) ?Event {\n   172        // Extract modifiers from param2 (CSI 1;2A = Shift+Up, etc.)\n   173        const mods = modifiersFromParam(param2);\n   174\n   175        return switch (final) {\n   176            'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up, .modifiers = mods } },\n   177            'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down, .modifiers = mods } },\n   178            'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right, .modifiers = mods } },\n   179            'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left, .modifiers = mods } },\n   180            'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n   181            'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n   182            '~' => switch (param1) {\n   183                1 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n   184                2 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .insert, .modifiers = mods } },\n   185                3 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .delete, .modifiers = mods } },\n   186                4 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n   187                5 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .page_up, .modifiers = mods } },\n   188                6 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .page_down, .modifiers = mods } },\n   189                7 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n   190                8   17...21 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 11) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F6-F10\n   193                23, 24 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 12) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F11-F12\n   194                200 => null, // Bracketed paste start (handled elsewhere)\n   195                201 => null, // Bracketed paste end (handled elsewhere)\n   196                else => null,\n   197            },\n   198            'P' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 1 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F1\n   199            'Q' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 2 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F2\n   200            'R' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 3 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F3\n   201            'S' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 4 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F4\n   202            else => null,\n   203        };\n   204    }\n   205\n   206    /// Convert modifier parameter to Modifiers struct.\n   207    /// Terminal convention: 1=none, 2=shift, 3=alt, 4=shift+alt, 5=ctrl, etc.\n   208    fn modifiersFromParam(param: u16) Modifiers {\n   209        if (param == 0 or param == 1) {\n   210            return Modifiers{};\n   211        }\n   212\n   213        const p = param - 1;\n   214        return Modifiers{\n   215            .shift = (p & 1) != 0,\n   216            .alt = (p & 2) != 0,\n   217            .ctrl = (p & 4) != 0,\n   218        };\n   219    }\n   220\n   221    /// Parse an SS3 (Single Shift 3) sequence.\n   222    /// Used by some terminals for function keys and keypad.\n   223    fn parseSs3(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n   224        _ = self;\n   225        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n   226            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n   227        }\n   228\n   229        return switch (bytes[0]) {\n   230            'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up } },\n   231            'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down } },\n   232            'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right } },\n   233            'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left } },\n   234            'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home } },\n   235            'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end } },\n   236            'P' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 1 } } },\n   237            'Q' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 2 } } },\n   238            'R' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 3 } } },\n   239            'S' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 4 } } },\n   240            else => null,\n   241        };\n   242    }\n   243\n   244    /// Parse mouse sequences (X10 or SGR mode).\n   245    fn parseMouse(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n   246        _ = self;\n   247\n   248        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n   249            return null;\n   250        }\n   251\n   252        // SGR mode: ESC [ < Cb ; Cx ; Cy M/m\n   253        if (bytes[0] == '<') {\n   254            return parseMouseSgr(bytes[1..]);\n   255        }\n   256\n   257        // X10 mode: ESC [ M Cb Cx Cy\n   258        if (bytes[0] == 'M') {\n   259            return parseMouseX10(bytes[1..]);\n   260        }\n   261\n   262        return null;\n   263    }\n   264\n   265    /// Parse SGR mouse sequence.\n   266    /// Format: <Cb;Cx;Cy M or <Cb;Cx;Cy m\n   267    fn parseMouseSgr(bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n   268        var i: usize = 0;\n   269        var cb: u16 = 0;\n   270        var cx: u16 = 0;\n   271        var cy: u16 = 0;\n   272        var param_index: u8 = 0;\n   273\n   274        while (i < bytes.len) : (i += 1) {\n   275            const c = bytes[i];\n   276            if (c >= '0' and c <= '9') {\n   277                switch (param_index) {\n   278                    0 => cb = cb * 10 + (c - '0'),\n   279                    1 => cx = cx * 10 + (c - '0'),\n   280                    2 => cy = cy * 10 + (c - '0'),\n   281                    else => {},\n   282                }\n   283            } else if (c == ';') {\n   284                param_index += 1;\n   285            } else if (c == 'M' or c == 'm') {\n   286                // M = button press, m = button release\n   287                const is_release = (c == 'm');\n   288\n   289                // Decode button and modifiers from cb\n   290                const button = @as(u8, @intCast(cb & 0x03));\n   291                const shift = (cb & 0x04) != 0;\n   292                const alt = (cb & 0x08) != 0;\n   293                const ctrl = (cb & 0x10) != 0;\n   294                const motion = (cb & 0x20) != 0;\n   295                const wheel = (cb & 0x40) != 0;\n   296\n   297                const kind: MouseKind = if (wheel)\n   298                    if (button == 0) .scroll_up else .scroll_down\n   299                else if (motion)\n   300                    .drag\n   301                else if (is_release)\n   302                    .up\n   303                else\n   304                    .down;\n   305\n   306                // SGR coordinates are 1-based\n   307                const x = if (cx > 0) cx - 1 else 0;\n   308                const y = if (cy > 0) cy - 1 else 0;\n   309\n   310                return Event{\n   311                    .mouse = .{\n   312                        .x = x,\n   313                        .y = y,\n   314                        .kind = kind,\n   315                        .modifiers = .{\n   316                            .shift = shift,\n   317                            .alt = alt,\n   318                            .ctrl = ctrl,\n   319                        },\n   320                    },\n   321                };\n   322            }\n   323        }\n   324\n   325        return null;\n   326    }\n   327\n   328    /// Parse X10 mouse sequence.\n   329    /// Format: M Cb Cx Cy (all encoded as Cb+32, Cx+32, Cy+32)\n   330    fn parseMouseX10(bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n   331        if (bytes.len < 3) {\n   332            return null;\n   333        }\n   334\n   335        const cb = bytes[0] -| 32;\n   336        const cx = bytes[1] -| 32;\n   337        const cy = bytes[2] -| 32;\n   338\n   339        const button = cb & 0x03;\n   340        const shift = (cb & 0x04) != 0;\n   341        const alt = (cb & 0x08) != 0;\n   342        const ctrl = (cb & 0x10) != 0;\n   343        const motion = (cb & 0x20) != 0;\n   344        const wheel = (cb & 0x40) != 0;\n   345\n   346        const kind: MouseKind = if (wheel)\n   347            if (button == 0) .scroll_up else .scroll_down\n   348        else if (motion)\n   349            .drag\n   350        else if (button == 3)\n   351            .up // X10 uses button 3 for release\n   352        else\n   353            .down;\n   354\n   355        return Event{\n   356            .mouse = .{\n   357                .x = cx,\n   358                .y = cy,\n   359                .kind = kind,\n   360                .modifiers = .{\n   361                    .shift = shift,\n   362                    .alt = alt,\n   363                    .ctrl = ctrl,\n   364                },\n   365            },\n   366        };\n   367    }\n   368\n   369    /// Parse a paste sequence.\n   370    fn parsePaste(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n   371        // Look for paste end sequence: ESC [ 2 0 1 ~\n   372        const end_seq = \"\\x1b[201~\";\n   373        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, bytes, end_seq)) |_| {\n   374            self.in_paste = false;\n   375            // For now, we don't expose paste content as events\n   376            // Future: could return a paste event with content\n   377        }\n   378        return null;\n   379    }\n   380\n   381    /// Parse a UTF-8 character sequence.\n   382    fn parseUtf8(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n   383        _ = self;\n   384\n   385        // Determine UTF-8 sequence length from first byte\n   386        const len = utf8ByteLen(bytes[0]);\n   387\n   388        if (len == 0) {\n   389            return null;\n   390        }\n   391\n   392        if (bytes.len < len) {\n   393            // Incomplete sequence\n   394            return null;\n   395        }\n   396\n   397        // Decode the codepoint\n   398        const codepoint = std.unicode.utf8Decode(bytes[0..len]) catch {\n   399            return null;\n   400        };\n   401\n   402        return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = codepoint } } };\n   403    }\n   404};\n   405\n   406/// Get the length of a UTF-8 sequence from its first byte.\n   407fn utf8ByteLen(byte: u8) usize {\n   408    if (byte < 0x80) return 1;\n   409    if (byte < 0xc0) return 0; // Continuation byte\n   410    if (byte < 0xe0) return 2;\n   411    if (byte < 0xf0) return 3;\n   412    if (byte < 0xf8) return 4;\n   413    return 0;\n   414}\n   415\n   416// \"sanity: Input.init creates parser\" {\n   421    const input = Input.init();\n   422    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), input.buffer_len);\n   423    try Terminal input parsing for zithril TUI framework\n// Parses raw terminal bytes into Event types\n// Handles ANSI escape sequences for keys, mouse, and special characters\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst event_mod = @import(\"event.zig\");\n\npub const Event = event_mod.Event;\npub const Key = event_mod.Key;\npub const KeyCode = event_mod.KeyCode;\npub const Modifiers = event_mod.Modifiers;\npub const Mouse = event_mod.Mouse;\npub const MouseKind = event_mod.MouseKind;\npub const Size = event_mod.Size;\n\n/// Input parser state machine.\n/// Parses raw terminal input bytes into Event types.\npub const Input = struct {\n    /// Buffer for incomplete escape sequences\n    buffer: [32]u8 = undefined,\n    /// Number of bytes in buffer\n    buffer_len: usize = 0,\n    /// Whether we're in a paste sequence\n    in_paste: bool = false,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    /// Initialize a new input parser.\n    pub fn init() Self {\n        return .{};\n    }\n\n    /// Parse input bytes and return an event if one is complete.\n    /// May consume partial input for multi-byte sequences.\n    pub fn parse(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // Handle bracketed paste mode\n        if (self.in_paste) {\n            return self.parsePaste(bytes);\n        }\n\n        // Check for escape sequence\n        if (bytes[0] == 0x1b) {\n            return self.parseEscape(bytes);\n        }\n\n        // Handle control characters\n        if (bytes[0] < 0x20) {\n            return self.parseControl(bytes[0]);\n        }\n\n        // Handle regular UTF-8 character\n        return self.parseUtf8(bytes);\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a control character (0x00-0x1F).\n    fn parseControl(self: *Self, byte: u8) ?Event {\n        _ = self;\n        return switch (byte) {\n            0x00 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = ' ' }, .modifiers = .{ .ctrl = true } } }, // Ctrl+Space\n            0x09 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .tab } }, // Tab\n            0x0a, 0x0d => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .enter } }, // Enter (LF or CR)\n            0x7f => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .backspace } }, // Backspace (DEL)\n            // Ctrl+A through Ctrl+Z (excluding tab=0x09, enter=0x0a, and 0x0d)\n            0x01...0x08, 0x0b, 0x0c, 0x0e...0x1a => |b| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = 'a' + (b - 1) }, .modifiers = .{ .ctrl = true } } },\n            0x1b => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } }, // Escape (handled elsewhere)\n            else => null,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse an escape sequence.\n    fn parseEscape(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        if (bytes.len == 1) {\n            // Just ESC by itself\n            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n        }\n\n        const second = bytes[1];\n\n        // CSI sequence (ESC [)\n        if (second == '[') {\n            return self.parseCsi(bytes[2..]);\n        }\n\n        // SS3 sequence (ESC O)\n        if (second == 'O') {\n            return self.parseSs3(bytes[2..]);\n        }\n\n        // Alt+Escape\n        if (second == 0x1b) {\n            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape, .modifiers = .{ .alt = true } } };\n        }\n\n        // Alt+key (printable ASCII)\n        if (second >= 0x20 and second < 0x7f) {\n            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = second }, .modifiers = .{ .alt = true } } };\n        }\n\n        return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a CSI (Control Sequence Introducer) sequence.\n    /// Format: ESC [ <params> <final>\n    fn parseCsi(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n        }\n\n        // Check for mouse sequences\n        if (bytes[0] == 'M' or bytes[0] == '<') {\n            return self.parseMouse(bytes);\n        }\n\n        // Check for bracketed paste\n        if (bytes.len >= 4 and bytes[0] == '2' and bytes[1] == '0' and bytes[2] == '0' and bytes[3] == '~') {\n            self.in_paste = true;\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // Parse arrow keys and simple sequences\n        if (bytes.len >= 1) {\n            return switch (bytes[0]) {\n                'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up } },\n                'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down } },\n                'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right } },\n                'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left } },\n                'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home } },\n                'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end } },\n                'Z' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .backtab } }, // Shift+Tab\n                else => self.parseCsiParams(bytes),\n            };\n        }\n\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse CSI sequences with parameters.\n    fn parseCsiParams(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        _ = self;\n\n        // Find the final character\n        var i: usize = 0;\n        var param1: u16 = 0;\n        var param2: u16 = 0;\n        var in_second_param = false;\n\n        while (i < bytes.len) : (i += 1) {\n            const c = bytes[i];\n            if (c >= '0' and c <= '9') {\n                if (in_second_param) {\n                    param2 = param2 * 10 + (c - '0');\n                } else {\n                    param1 = param1 * 10 + (c - '0');\n                }\n            } else if (c == ';') {\n                in_second_param = true;\n            } else {\n                // Final character\n                return parseCsiFinal(c, param1, param2);\n            }\n        }\n\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse the final character of a CSI sequence.\n    fn parseCsiFinal(final: u8, param1: u16, param2: u16) ?Event {\n        // Extract modifiers from param2 (CSI 1;2A = Shift+Up, etc.)\n        const mods = modifiersFromParam(param2);\n\n        return switch (final) {\n            'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up, .modifiers = mods } },\n            'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down, .modifiers = mods } },\n            'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right, .modifiers = mods } },\n            'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left, .modifiers = mods } },\n            'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n            'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n            '~' => switch (param1) {\n                1 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n                2 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .insert, .modifiers = mods } },\n                3 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .delete, .modifiers = mods } },\n                4 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n                5 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .page_up, .modifiers = mods } },\n                6 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .page_down, .modifiers = mods } },\n                7 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n                8 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n                11...15 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 10) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F1-F5\n                17...21 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 11) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F6-F10\n                23, 24 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 12) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F11-F12\n                200 => null, // Bracketed paste start (handled elsewhere)\n                201 => null, // Bracketed paste end (handled elsewhere)\n                else => null,\n            },\n            'P' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 1 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F1\n            'Q' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 2 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F2\n            'R' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 3 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F3\n            'S' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 4 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F4\n            else => null,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Convert modifier parameter to Modifiers struct.\n    /// Terminal convention: 1=none, 2=shift, 3=alt, 4=shift+alt, 5=ctrl, etc.\n    fn modifiersFromParam(param: u16) Modifiers {\n        if (param == 0 or param == 1) {\n            return Modifiers{};\n        }\n\n        const p = param - 1;\n        return Modifiers{\n            .shift = (p & 1) != 0,\n            .alt = (p & 2) != 0,\n            .ctrl = (p & 4) != 0,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse an SS3 (Single Shift 3) sequence.\n    /// Used by some terminals for function keys and keypad.\n    fn parseSs3(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        _ = self;\n        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n        }\n\n        return switch (bytes[0]) {\n            'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up } },\n            'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down } },\n            'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right } },\n            'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left } },\n            'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home } },\n            'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end } },\n            'P' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 1 } } },\n            'Q' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 2 } } },\n            'R' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 3 } } },\n            'S' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 4 } } },\n            else => null,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse mouse sequences (X10 or SGR mode).\n    fn parseMouse(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        _ = self;\n\n        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // SGR mode: ESC [ < Cb ; Cx ; Cy M/m\n        if (bytes[0] == '<') {\n            return parseMouseSgr(bytes[1..]);\n        }\n\n        // X10 mode: ESC [ M Cb Cx Cy\n        if (bytes[0] == 'M') {\n            return parseMouseX10(bytes[1..]);\n        }\n\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse SGR mouse sequence.\n    /// Format: <Cb;Cx;Cy M or <Cb;Cx;Cy m\n    fn parseMouseSgr(bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        var i: usize = 0;\n        var cb: u16 = 0;\n        var cx: u16 = 0;\n        var cy: u16 = 0;\n        var param_index: u8 = 0;\n\n        while (i < bytes.len) : (i += 1) {\n            const c = bytes[i];\n            if (c >= '0' and c <= '9') {\n                switch (param_index) {\n                    0 => cb = cb * 10 + (c - '0'),\n                    1 => cx = cx * 10 + (c - '0'),\n                    2 => cy = cy * 10 + (c - '0'),\n                    else => {},\n                }\n            } else if (c == ';') {\n                param_index += 1;\n            } else if (c == 'M' or c == 'm') {\n                // M = button press, m = button release\n                const is_release = (c == 'm');\n\n                // Decode button and modifiers from cb\n                const button = @as(u8, @intCast(cb & 0x03));\n                const shift = (cb & 0x04) != 0;\n                const alt = (cb & 0x08) != 0;\n                const ctrl = (cb & 0x10) != 0;\n                const motion = (cb & 0x20) != 0;\n                const wheel = (cb & 0x40) != 0;\n\n                const kind: MouseKind = if (wheel)\n                    if (button == 0) .scroll_up else .scroll_down\n                else if (motion)\n                    .drag\n                else if (is_release)\n                    .up\n                else\n                    .down;\n\n                // SGR coordinates are 1-based\n                const x = if (cx > 0) cx - 1 else 0;\n                const y = if (cy > 0) cy - 1 else 0;\n\n                return Event{\n                    .mouse = .{\n                        .x = x,\n                        .y = y,\n                        .kind = kind,\n                        .modifiers = .{\n                            .shift = shift,\n                            .alt = alt,\n                            .ctrl = ctrl,\n                        },\n                    },\n                };\n            }\n        }\n\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse X10 mouse sequence.\n    /// Format: M Cb Cx Cy (all encoded as Cb+32, Cx+32, Cy+32)\n    fn parseMouseX10(bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        if (bytes.len < 3) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        const cb = bytes[0] -| 32;\n        const cx = bytes[1] -| 32;\n        const cy = bytes[2] -| 32;\n\n        const button = cb & 0x03;\n        const shift = (cb & 0x04) != 0;\n        const alt = (cb & 0x08) != 0;\n        const ctrl = (cb & 0x10) != 0;\n        const motion = (cb & 0x20) != 0;\n        const wheel = (cb & 0x40) != 0;\n\n        const kind: MouseKind = if (wheel)\n            if (button == 0) .scroll_up else .scroll_down\n        else if (motion)\n            .drag\n        else if (button == 3)\n            .up // X10 uses button 3 for release\n        else\n            .down;\n\n        return Event{\n            .mouse = .{\n                .x = cx,\n                .y = cy,\n                .kind = kind,\n                .modifiers = .{\n                    .shift = shift,\n                    .alt = alt,\n                    .ctrl = ctrl,\n                },\n            },\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a paste sequence.\n    fn parsePaste(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        // Look for paste end sequence: ESC [ 2 0 1 ~\n        const end_seq = \"\\x1b[201~\";\n        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, bytes, end_seq)) |_| {\n            self.in_paste = false;\n            // For now, we don't expose paste content as events\n            // Future: could return a paste event with content\n        }\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a UTF-8 character sequence.\n    fn parseUtf8(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        _ = self;\n\n        // Determine UTF-8 sequence length from first byte\n        const len = utf8ByteLen(bytes[0]);\n\n        if (len == 0) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        if (bytes.len < len) {\n            // Incomplete sequence\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // Decode the codepoint\n        const codepoint = std.unicode.utf8Decode(bytes[0..len]) catch {\n            return null;\n        };\n\n        return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = codepoint } } };\n    }\n};\n\n/// Get the length of a UTF-8 sequence from its first byte.\nfn utf8ByteLen(byte: u8) usize {\n    if (byte < 0x80) return 1;\n    if (byte < 0xc0) return 0; // Continuation byte\n    if (byte < 0xe0) return 2;\n    if (byte < 0xf0) return 3;\n    if (byte < 0xf8) return 4;\n    return 0;\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic input parsing\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: Input.init creates parser\" {\n    const input = Input.init();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), input.buffer_len);\n    try std.testing.expect(!input.in_paste);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: parse single ASCII character\" {\n    var input = Input.init();\n    const event = input.parse(\"a\");\n    try std.testing.expect(event != null);\n    try std.testing.expect(event.? == .key);\n    try std.testing.expect(event.?.key.code == .char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'a'), event.?.key.code.char);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: parse escape key\" {\n    var input = Input.init();\n    const event = input.parse(\"\\x1b\");\n    try std.testing.expect(event != null);\n    try std.testing.expect(event.?.key.code == .escape);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: parse enter key\" {\n    var input = Input.init();\n    const event = input.parse(\"\\r\");\n    try std.testing.expect(event !=       return .{\n   101                .alternate_screen = self.alternate_screen,\n   102                .hide_cursor = true,\n   103                .mouse_capture = self.mouse_capture,\n   104 Repeat\n   138        pub fn run(self: *Self, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) RunError!void {\n   139            // Initialize terminal backend\n   140            var backend = error.TerminalQueryFailed => RunError.TerminalQueryFailed,\n   144                    error.TerminalSetFailed => RunError.TerminalSetFailed,\n   145                    error.IoError =>           };\n   165            defer previous_buf.deinit();\n   166\n   167            // Allocate update buffer for diff results\n   168            const max_updates = @as(usize, initial_size.width) * @as(usize, initial_size.height);\n   169            var updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, max_updates) catch {\n   170                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n   171            };\n   172            defer allocator.free(updates);\n   173\n   174            // Calculate tick timeout in nanoseconds (0 means no timeout/poll mode)\n   175            const tick_timeout_ns: ?u64 =  backend.cursorHome();\n   186\n   187            // Initial render\n   188            {\n   189                current_buf.clear();\n   190                var frame = current_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n   223                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n   224                    };\n   225                    previous_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n   226                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n   227                    };\n   228\n   229                    allocator.free(updates);\n   230                    updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, new_max_updates) catch {\n   231                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n   232 self.view(&frame);\n   253\n   254                // Render changes to terminal\n   255                try renderBuffer(&backend, &current_buf, &previous_buf, updates);\n   256\n   257                // Swap buffers (copy current to previous for next diff)\n   258                @memcpy(previous_buf.cells, current_buf.cells);\n   259            }\n   260        }\n   261\n   262        /// Poll for an input event from the terminal.\n   263        /// Returns null if no event is available within the timeout.\n   264        fn pollEvent(input: *Input, backend: *Backend, timeout_ns: ?u64)   278            }\n   279\n   280            // Parse input bytes into events\n   281            if (input.parse(buf[0..bytes_read])) |parsed_event| {\n   282                _ = backend; // Backend used for future resize detection\n   283                return parsed_event;\n   284            }\n   285\n   286            return null;\n   287        }\n   288\n   289        /// Render buffer update_buffer: []buffer_mod.CellUpdate,\n   295        ) RunError!void {\n   296            const changes = current.diff(previous.*, update_buffer);\n   297\n   298            if (changes.len == 0) {\n   299                return;\n   300            }\n   301\n   302            // Build output string with cursor movements and cell contents\n   303            var output_buf: [8192]u8 = undefined;\n   304            var output_len: usize = 0;\n   305\n   306            var last_x: ?u16 = null;\n   307            var last_y: ?u16 = null;\n   308\n   309            for (changes) |change| {\n   310                // Move cursor if not consecutive\n   311                const need_move = if (last_x == null or last_y == null)\n   312                    true\n   313                else if (last_y.? != change.y)\n   314                    true\n   315                else if (last_x.? + 1 != change.x)\n   316                    true\n   317                else\n   318                    false;\n   319\n   320                if (need_move) {\n   321                    // Add cursor position escape sequence\n   322                    const move_seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(\n   323                        output_buf[output_len..],\n   324                        \"\\x1b[{d};{d}H\",\n   325                        .{ change.y + 1, change.x + 1 },\n   326                    ) catch style_seq.len;\n   336\n   337                // Add character\n   338                if (change.cell.width > 0) {\n   339                    var char_buf: [4]u8 = undefined;\n   340 output_buf.len) {\n   353                @memcpy(output_buf[output_len..][0..4], \"\\x1b[0m\");\n   354                output_len += 4;\n   355            }\n   356\n   357            // Write to terminal\n   358            backend.write(output_buf[0..output_len]) catch {\n   359                return RunError.IoError;\n   360            };\n   361            backend.flush();\n   362        }\n   363\n   364        /// Render a cell's style as an ANSI escape sequence.\n   365        fn renderCellStyle(buf: []u8, cell: cell_mod.Cell) error{NoSpaceLeft}![]u8 {\n   366            const style = cell.style;\n   367\n   368            // Use a fixed-size buffer for building the escape sequence\n   369            var fbs = std.io.fixedBufferStream(buf);\n   370            const writer = style.inner.foreground;\n   400            if (!fg.eql(@import(\"rich_zig\").Color.default)) {\n   401                if (fg.color_type == .standard or fg.color_type == .eight_bit) {\n   402   try writer.print(\";38;2;{d};{d};{d}\", .{ t.r, t.g, t.b });\n   414                    }\n   415                }\n   416            }\n   417\n   418            // Add background color if set\n   419            const bg = style.inner.background;\n   420            if (!bg.eql(@import(\"rich_zig\").Color.default)) {\n   421                if (bg.color_type == .standard or bg.color_type == App runtime for zithril TUI framework\n// Generic application type parameterized by user state\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst frame_mod = @import(\"frame.zig\");\nconst event_mod = @import(\"event.zig\");\nconst action_mod = @import(\"action.zig\");\nconst buffer_mod = @import(\"buffer.zig\");\nconst backend_mod = @import(\"backend.zig\");\nconst input_mod = @import(\"input.zig\");\nconst cell_mod = @import(\"cell.zig\");\n\npub const Frame = frame_mod.Frame;\npub const Event = event_mod.Event;\npub const Action = action_mod.Action;\npub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\npub const Backend = backend_mod.Backend;\npub const Input = input_mod.Input;\n\n/// App is the main runtime type, generic over the user's state type.\n/// The user provides their own State struct and function pointers for update and view.\n///\n/// Fields:\n/// - state: Instance of the user's State type\n/// - update_fn: Function pointer for handling events, returns an Action\n/// - view_fn: Function pointer for rendering the UI\n/// - tick_rate_ms: Timer interval for tick events (0 = disabled)\n/// - mouse_capture: Enable mouse event reporting\n/// - paste_bracket: Enable bracketed paste mode\n/// - alternate_screen: Use alternate screen buffer\npub fn App(comptime State: type) type {\n    return struct {\n        const Self = @This();\n\n        /// Default max widgets for frame layout cache.\n        pub const DefaultMaxWidgets: usize = 64;\n\n        /// User-defined state instance.\n        state: State,\n\n        /// Update function: receives state and event, returns an Action.\n        /// Signature: fn(*State, Event) Action\n        update_fn: *const fn (*State, Event) Action,\n\n        /// View function: receives state and frame, renders the UI.\n        /// Signature: fn(*State, *Frame(N)) void\n        /// The frame provides layout and render methods.\n        view_fn: *const fn (*State, *Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets)) void,\n\n        /// Timer interval in milliseconds for tick events.\n        /// Set to 0 to disable tick events.\n        tick_rate_ms: u32,\n\n        /// Enable mouse event reporting.\n        /// When true, the terminal backend will capture mouse events.\n        mouse_capture: bool,\n\n        /// Enable bracketed paste mode.\n        /// Distinguishes pasted text from typed text.\n        paste_bracket: bool,\n\n        /// Use alternate screen buffer.\n        /// Preserves original terminal content on exit.\n        alternate_screen: bool,\n\n        /// Configuration options for App initialization.\n        pub const Config = struct {\n            /// Initial state instance.\n            state: State,\n            /// Update function pointer.\n            update: *const fn (*State, Event) Action,\n            /// View function pointer.\n            view: *const fn (*State, *Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets)) void,\n            /// Timer interval in milliseconds for tick events (0 = disabled).\n            tick_rate_ms: u32 = 0,\n            /// Enable mouse event reporting.\n            mouse_capture: bool = false,\n            /// Enable bracketed paste mode.\n            paste_bracket: bool = false,\n            /// Use alternate screen buffer.\n            alternate_screen: bool = true,\n        };\n\n        /// Initialize an App with the given configuration.\n        pub fn init(config: Config) Self {\n            return .{\n                .state = config.state,\n                .update_fn = config.update,\n                .view_fn = config.view,\n                .tick_rate_ms = config.tick_rate_ms,\n                .mouse_capture = config.mouse_capture,\n                .paste_bracket = config.paste_bracket,\n                .alternate_screen = config.alternate_screen,\n            };\n        }\n\n        /// Returns a BackendConfig derived from this App's configuration.\n        /// Used by the event loop to initialize the terminal backend.\n        pub fn backendConfig(self: Self) @import(\"backend.zig\").BackendConfig {\n            return .{\n                .alternate_screen = self.alternate_screen,\n                .hide_cursor = true,\n                .mouse_capture = self.mouse_capture,\n                .bracketed_paste = self.paste_bracket,\n            };\n        }\n\n        /// Call the update function with an event.\n        /// Returns the action to be processed by the runtime.\n        pub fn update(self: *Self, event: Event) Action {\n            return self.update_fn(&self.state, event);\n        }\n\n        /// Call the view function with a frame.\n        /// The view function should use frame.render() to draw widgets.\n        pub fn view(self: *Self, frame: *Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets)) void {\n            self.view_fn(&self.state, frame);\n        }\n\n        /// Error type for run operations.\n        pub const RunError = error{\n            OutOfMemory,\n            NotATty,\n            TerminalQueryFailed,\n            TerminalSetFailed,\n            IoError,\n        };\n\n        /// Run the main event loop until Action.quit is returned.\n        ///\n        /// Main loop:\n        /// 1. Poll for events (keyboard, mouse, resize, or tick timeout)\n        /// 2. Call update function with the event\n        /// 3. Check action - if .quit, exit loop\n        /// 4. Call view function to describe the UI\n        /// 5. Render by diffing buffers and writing changes to terminal\n        /// 6. Repeat\n        pub fn run(self: *Self, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) RunError!void {\n            // Initialize terminal backend\n            var backend = Backend.init(self.backendConfig()) catch |err| {\n                return switch (err) {\n                    error.NotATty => RunError.NotATty,\n                    error.TerminalQueryFailed => RunError.TerminalQueryFailed,\n                    error.TerminalSetFailed => RunError.TerminalSetFailed,\n                    error.IoError => RunError.IoError,\n                };\n            };\n            defer backend.deinit();\n\n            // Initialize input parser\n            var input = Input.init();\n\n            // Get initial terminal size\n            const initial_size = backend.getSize();\n\n            // Create double buffers for diffing\n            var current_buf = Buffer.init(allocator, initial_size.width, initial_size.height) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer current_buf.deinit();\n\n            var previous_buf = Buffer.init(allocator, initial_size.width, initial_size.height) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer previous_buf.deinit();\n\n            // Allocate update buffer for diff results\n            const max_updates = @as(usize, initial_size.width) * @as(usize, initial_size.height);\n            var updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, max_updates) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer allocator.free(updates);\n\n            // Calculate tick timeout in nanoseconds (0 means no timeout/poll mode)\n            const tick_timeout_ns: ?u64 = if (self.tick_rate_ms > 0)\n                @as(u64, self.tick_rate_ms) * std.time.ns_per_ms\n            else\n                null;\n\n            // Track last tick time for tick events\n            var last_tick: i128 = std.time.nanoTimestamp();\n\n            // Clear screen initially\n            backend.clearScreen();\n            backend.cursorHome();\n\n            // Initial render\n            {\n                current_buf.clear();\n                var frame = Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets).init(&current_buf);\n                self.view(&frame);\n                try renderBuffer(&backend, &current_buf, &previous_buf, updates);\n                @memcpy(previous_buf.cells, current_buf.cells);\n            }\n\n            // Main event loop\n            while (true) {\n                // Poll for events or wait for tick timeout\n                const maybe_event = try pollEvent(&input, &backend, tick_timeout_ns);\n\n                // Handle tick event generation\n                var event: Event = undefined;\n                if (maybe_event) |e| {\n                    event = e;\n                } else if (tick_timeout_ns != null) {\n                    const now = std.time.nanoTimestamp();\n                    if (now - last_tick >= @as(i128, tick_timeout_ns.?)) {\n                        event = Event{ .tick = {} };\n                        last_tick = now;\n                    } else {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                // Handle resize events specially - resize buffers\n                if (event == .resize) {\n                    const new_size = event.resize;\n                    const new_max_updates = @as(usize, new_size.width) * @as(usize, new_size.height);\n\n                    current_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n                    previous_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n\n                    allocator.free(updates);\n                    updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, new_max_updates) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n\n                    // Clear screen on resize\n                    backend.clearScreen();\n                    backend.cursorHome();\n                }\n\n                // Call update function\n                const action = self.update(event);\n\n                // Check for quit action\n                if (action.isQuit()) {\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                // TODO: Handle command actions in the future\n\n                // Clear current buffer and call view function\n                current_buf.clear();\n                var frame = Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets).init(&current_buf);\n                self.view(&frame);\n\n                // Render changes to terminal\n                try renderBuffer(&backend, &current_buf, &previous_buf, updates);\n\n                // Swap buffers (copy current to previous for next diff)\n                @memcpy(previous_buf.cells, current_buf.cells);\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// Poll for an input event from the terminal.\n        /// Returns null if no event is available within the timeout.\n        fn pollEvent(input: *Input, backend: *Backend, timeout_ns: ?u64) RunError!?Event {\n            _ = timeout_ns; // TODO: Implement proper polling with timeout\n\n            // Read available input bytes\n            var buf: [256]u8 = undefined;\n            const bytes_read = std.posix.read(std.posix.STDIN_FILENO, &buf) catch |err| {\n                switch (err) {\n                    error.WouldBlock => return null,\n                    else => return RunError.IoError,\n                }\n            };\n\n            if (bytes_read == 0) {\n                return null;\n            }\n\n            // Parse input bytes into events\n            if (input.parse(buf[0..bytes_read])) |parsed_event| {\n                _ = backend; // Backend used for future resize detection\n                return parsed_event;\n            }\n\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        /// Render buffer changes to the terminal.\n        fn renderBuffer(\n            backend: *Backend,\n            current: *Buffer,\n            previous: *Buffer,\n            update_buffer: []buffer_mod.CellUpdate,\n        ) RunError!void {\n            const changes = current.diff(previous.*, update_buffer);\n\n            if (changes.len == 0) {\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // Build output string with cursor movements and cell contents\n            var output_buf: [8192]u8 = undefined;\n            var output_len: usize = 0;\n\n            var last_x: ?u16 = null;\n            var last_y: ?u16 = null;\n\n            for (changes) |change| {\n                // Move cursor if not consecutive\n                const need_move = if (last_x == null or last_y == null)\n                    true\n                else if (last_y.? != change.y)\n                    true\n                else if (last_x.? + 1 != change.x)\n                    true\n                else\n                    false;\n\n                if (need_move) {\n                    // Add cursor position escape sequence\n                    const move_seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(\n                        output_buf[output_len..],\n                        \"\\x1b[{d};{d}H\",\n                        .{ change.y + 1, change.x + 1 },\n                    ) catch break;\n                    output_len += move_seq.len;\n                }\n\n                // Add style escape sequence\n                const style_seq = renderCellStyle(\n                    output_buf[output_len..],\n                    change.cell,\n                ) catch break;\n                output_len += style_seq.len;\n\n                // Add character\n                if (change.cell.width > 0) {\n                    var char_buf: [4]u8 = undefined;\n                    const char_len = std.unicode.utf8Encode(change.cell.char, &char_buf) catch 1;\n                    if (output_len + char_len <= output_buf.len) {\n                        @memcpy(output_buf[output_len..][0..char_len], char_buf[0..char_len]);\n                        output_len += char_len;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                last_x = change.x;\n                last_y = change.y;\n            }\n\n            // Reset style at the end\n            if (output_len + 4 <= output_buf.len) {\n                @memcpy(output_buf[output_len..][0..4], \"\\x1b[0m\");\n                output_len += 4;\n            }\n\n            // Write to terminal\n            backend.write(output_buf[0..output_len]) catch {\n                return RunError.IoError;\n            };\n            backend.flush();\n        }\n\n        /// Render a cell's style as an ANSI escape sequence.\n        fn renderCellStyle(buf: []u8, cell: cell_mod.Cell) error{NoSpaceLeft}![]u8 {\n            const style = cell.style;\n\n            // Use a fixed-size buffer for building the escape sequence\n            var fbs = std.io.fixedBufferStream(buf);\n            const writer = fbs.writer();\n\n            // Write SGR introducer\n            try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b[0\");\n\n            // Add attributes\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.bold)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";1\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.dim)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";2\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.italic)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";3\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.underline)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";4\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.blink)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";5\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.reverse)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";7\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.strike)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";9\");\n            }\n\n            // Add foreground color if set\n            const fg = style.inner.foreground;\n            if (!fg.eql(@import(\"rich_zig\").Color.default)) {\n                if (fg.color_type == .standard or fg.color_type == .eight_bit) {\n                    if (fg.number) |n| {\n                        if (n < 8) {\n                            try writer.print(\";{d}\", .{30 + n});\n                        } else if (n < 16) {\n                            try writer.print(\";{d}\", .{90 + n - 8});\n                        } else {\n                            try writer.print(\";38;5;{d}\", .{n});\n                        }\n                    }\n                } else if (fg.color_type == .truecolor) {\n                    if (fg.triplet) |t| {\n                        try writer.print(\";38;2;{d};{d};{d}\", .{ t.r, t.g, t.b });\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Add background color if set\n            const bg = style.inner.background;\n            if (!bg.eql(@import(\"rich_zig\").Color.default)) {\n                if (bg.color_type == .standard or bg.color_type == .eight_bit) {\n                    if (bg.number) |n| {\n                        if (n < 8) {\n                            try writer.print(\";{d}\", .{40 + n});\n                        } else if (n < 16) {\n                            try writer.print(\";{d}\", .{100 + n - 8});\n .truecolor) {\n                    if (bg.triplet) |t| {\n                        try writer.print(\";48;2;{d};{d};{d}\", .{ t.r, t.g, t.b });\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            try writer.writeByte('m');\n\n            return fbs.getWritten();\n        }\n    };\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic
