}\n    36        if (config.alternate_screen) {\n    37            file.writeAll(\"\\x1b[?1049l\") catch {};\n    38        }\n    39    }\n    40\n    41    // Restore termios\n    42    if (emergency_original_termios) |original| {\n    43        posix.tcsetattr(fd, .FLUSH, original) catch {};\n    44    }\n    45\n    46    // Clear global state\n    47    global_backend = null;\n    48    emergency_original_termios = null;\n    49    emergency_config = null;\n    50}\n    51\n    52/// Panic handler namespace for terminal cleanup.\n    53/// Applications can use this by adding to their root source file:\n    54///   pub const panic = @import(\"zithril\").backend_mod.panic;\n    55/// This ensures terminal state is restored before panic output is displayed.\n    56pub const panic = struct {\n    57    /// Core panic function called by @panic and runtime safety checks.\n    58    pub fn call(msg: []const u8, ret_addr: ?usize) noreturn {\n    59        @branchHint(.cold);\n    60        // Perform cleanup first so panic message is visible\n    61        emergencyCleanup();\n    62\n    63        // Use standard panic behavior\n    64        _ = ret_addr;\n    65        std.debug.lockStdErr();\n    66        const stderr = std.io.getStdErr();\n    67        stderr.writeAll(msg) catch {};\n    68        stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\") catch {};\n    69        @trap();\n    70    }\n    71\n    72    pub fn sentinelMismatch(expected: anytype, found: @TypeOf(expected)) noreturn {\n    73        _ = found;\n    74        call(\"sentinel mismatch\", null);\n    75    }\n    76\n    77    pub fn unwrapError(err: anyerror) noreturn {\n    78        _ = &err;\n    79        call(\"attempt to unwrap error\", null);\n    80    }\n    81\n    82    pub fn outOfBounds(index: usize, len: usize) noreturn {\n    83        _ = index;\n    84        _ = len;\n    85        call(\"index out of bounds\", null);\n    86    }\n    87\n    88    pub fn startGreaterThanEnd(start: usize, end: usize) noreturn {\n    89        _ = start;\n    90        _ = end;\n    91        call(\"start index is larger than end index\", null);\n    92    }\n    93\n    94    pub fn inactiveUnionField(active: anytype, accessed: @TypeOf(active)) noreturn {\n    95        _ = accessed;\n    96        call(\"access of inactive union field\", null);\n    97    }\n    98\n    99    pub fn sliceCastLenRemainder(src_len: usize) noreturn {\n   100        _ = src_len;\n   101        call(\"slice cast has len remainder\", null);\n   102    }\n   103\n   104    pub fn castToNull(value: anytype) noreturn {\n   105        _ = value;\n   106        call(\"cast to null\", null);\n   107    }\n   108\n   109    pub fn reachedUnreachable() noreturn {\n   110        call(\"reached unreachable code\", null);\n   111    }\n   112\n   113    pub fn unwrapNull() noreturn {\n   114        call(\"unwrap of null optional\", null);\n   115    }\n   116\n   117    pub fn signedOverflow(a: anytype, b: anytype) noreturn {\n   118        _ = a;\n   119        _ = b;\n   120        call(\"signed integer overflow\", null);\n   121    }\n   122\n   123    pub fn unsignedOverflow(a: anytype, b: anytype) noreturn {\n   124        _ = a;\n   125        _ = b;\n   126        call(\"unsigned integer overflow\", null);\n   127    }\n   128\n   129    pub fn exactDivisionRemainder(numerator: anytype, denominator: anytype) noreturn {\n   130        _ = numerator;\n   131        _ = denominator;\n   132        call(\"exact division has remainder\", null);\n   133    }\n   134\n   135    pub fn divisionByZero(numerator: anytype) noreturn {\n   136        _ = numerator;\n   137        call(\"division by zero\", null);\n   138    }\n   139\n   140    pub fn negativeShiftCount(count: anytype) noreturn {\n   141        _ = count;\n   142        call(\"negative shift count\", null);\n   143    }\n   144\n   145    pub fn shiftOverflow(a: anytype, b: anytype) noreturn {\n   146        _ = a;\n   147        _ = b;\n   148        call(\"shift overflow\", null);\n   149    }\n   150\n   151    pub fn memcpyDestOverlap() noreturn {\n   152        call(\"memcpy dest overlaps src\", null);\n   153    }\n   154\n   155    pub fn intToEnumOverflow() noreturn {\n   156        call(\"int to enum overflow\", null);\n   157    }\n   158\n   159    pub fn intToFloatOverflow(value: anytype) noreturn {\n   160        _ = value;\n   161        call(\"int to float overflow\", null);\n   162    }\n   163\n   164    pub fn floatToIntOverflow(value: anytype) noreturn {\n   165        _ = value;\n   166        call(\"float to int overflow\", null);\n   167    }\n   168\n   169    pub fn invalidEnumCast(value: anytype) noreturn {\n   170        _ = value;\n   171        call(\"invalid enum cast\", null);\n   172    }\n   173\n   174    pub fn noReturn() noreturn {\n   175        call(\"noreturn function returned\", null);\n   176    }\n   177};\n   178\n   179/// Color support levels detected from terminal capabilities.\n   180pub const ColorSupport = enum {\n   181    /// Basic 8/16 colors (standard ANSI).\n   182    basic,\n   183    /// 256 color palette (xterm-256color).\n   184    extended,\n   185    /// 24-bit true color (RGB).\n   186    true_color,\n   187\n   188    /// Returns the number of colors supported.\n   189    pub fn colorCount(self: ColorSupport) u32 {\n   190        return switch (self) {\n   191            .basic => 16,\n   192            .extended => 256,\n   193            .true_color => 16_777_216,\n   194        };\n   195    }\n   196\n   197    /// Returns true if this support level includes the given level.\n   198    pub fn supports(self: ColorSupport, level: ColorSupport) bool {\n   199        return @intFromEnum(self) >= @intFromEnum(level);\n   200    }\n   201};\n   202\n   203/// Terminal size in cells.\n   204pub const TerminalSize = struct {\n   205    width: u16,\n   206    height: u16,\n   207};\n   208\n   209/// Configuration options for terminal initialization.\n   210pub const BackendConfig = struct {\n   211    /// Enter alternate screen buffer (preserves original terminal content).\n   212    alternate_screen: bool = true,\n   213    /// Hide cursor during TUI operation.\n   214    hide_cursor: bool = true,\n   215    /// Enable mouse event reporting.\n   216    mouse_capture: bool = false,\n   217    /// Enable bracketed paste mode (distinguish pasted text from typed).\n   218    bracketed_paste: bool = false,\n   219};\n   220\n   221/// Terminal backend state.\n   222/// Manages raw mode, alternate screen, and other terminal features.\n   223/// RAII pattern: deinit() restores terminal to original state.\n   224pub const Backend = struct {\n   225    /// File descriptor for terminal output (typically stdout).\n   226    fd: posix.fd_t,\n   227    /// Original terminal settings, saved for restoration.\n   228    original_termios: ?posix.termios,\n   229    /// Configuration used during initialization.\n   230    config: BackendConfig,\n   231    /// Whether the backend is currently active.\n   232    active: bool,\n   233\n   234    /// Error type for backend operations.\n   235    pub const Error = error{\n   236        NotATty,\n   237        TerminalQueryFailed,\n   238        TerminalSetFailed,\n   239        IoError,\n   240    };\n   241\n   242    /// Initialize the terminal backend.\n   243    /// Enables raw mode and optional features based on config.\n   244    /// Registers panic handler to ensure cleanup on abnormal exit.\n   245    /// Returns error if stdout is not a TTY or terminal ops fail.\n   246    pub fn init(config: BackendConfig) Error!Backend {\n   247        const fd = posix.STDOUT_FILENO;\n   248\n   249        if (!posix.isatty(fd)) {\n   250            return Error.NotATty;\n   251        }\n   252\n   253        var self = Backend{\n   254            .fd = fd,\n   255            .original_termios = null,\n   256            .config = config,\n   257            .active = false,\n   258        };\n   259\n   260        try self.enterRawMode();\n   261        self.active = true;\n   262\n   263        // Store state for emergency cleanup\n   264        emergency_original_termios = self.original_termios;\n   265        emergency_config = config;\n   266        global_backend = &self;\n   267\n   268        if (config.alternate_screen) {\n   269            self.writeEscape(ENTER_ALTERNATE_SCREEN);\n   270        }\n   271\n   272        if (config.hide_cursor) {\n   273            self.writeEscape(HIDE_CURSOR);\n   274        }\n   275\n   276        if (config.mouse_capture) {\n   277            self.enableMouse();\n   278        }\n   279\n   280        if (config.bracketed_paste) {\n   281            self.writeEscape(ENABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE);\n   282        }\n   283\n   284        return self;\n   285    }\n   286\n   287    /// Restore terminal to original state.\n   288    /// Disables bracketed paste, mouse capture, shows cursor, leaves alternate screen,\n   289    /// and restores raw mode settings.\n   290    /// Safe to call multiple times.\n   291    pub fn deinit(self: *Backend) void {\n   292        if (!self.active) return;\n   293\n   294        // Disable bracketed paste\n   295        if (self.config.bracketed_paste) {\n   296            self.writeEscape(DISABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE);\n   297        }\n   298\n   299        // Disable mouse capture\n   300        if (self.config.mouse_capture) {\n   301            self.disableMouse();\n   302        }\n   303\n   304        // Show cursor\n   305        if (self.config.hide_cursor) {\n   306            self.writeEscape(SHOW_CURSOR);\n   307        }\n   308\n   309        // Leave alternate screen\n   310        if (self.config.alternate_screen) {\n   311            self.writeEscape(LEAVE_ALTERNATE_SCREEN);\n   312        }\n   313\n   314        // Restore raw mode (disable raw mode)\n   315        self.exitRawMode();\n   316        self.active = false;\n   317\n   318        // Clear global state for panic handler\n   319        if (global_backend == self) {\n   320            global_backend = null;\n   321            emergency_original_termios = null;\n   322            emergency_config = null;\n   323        }\n   324    }\n   325\n   326    /// Enter raw mode: disable line buffering, echo, and canonical mode.\n   327    fn enterRawMode(self: *Backend) Error!void {\n   328        const original = posix.tcgetattr(self.fd) catch {\n   329            return Error.TerminalQueryFailed;\n   330        };\n   331        self.original_termios = original;\n   332\n   333        var raw = original;\n   334\n   335        // Input flags: disable break handling, CR-to-NL, parity, strip, flow control\n   336        raw.iflag.BRKINT = false;\n   337        raw.iflag.ICRNL = false;\n   338        raw.iflag.INPCK = false;\n   339        raw.iflag.ISTRIP = false;\n   340        raw.iflag.IXON = false;\n   341\n   342        // Output flags: disable post-processing\n   343        raw.oflag.OPOST = false;\n   344\n   345        // Control flags: set character size to 8 bits\n   346        raw.cflag.CSIZE = .CS8;\n   347\n   348        // Local flags: disable echo, canonical mode, signals, extended input\n   349        raw.lflag.ECHO = false;\n   350        raw.lflag.ICANON = false;\n   351        raw.lflag.ISIG = false;\n   352        raw.lflag.IEXTEN = false;\n   353\n   354        // Set minimum chars for non-canonical read\n   355        raw.cc[@intFromEnum(posix.V.MIN)] = 0;\n   356        raw.cc[@intFromEnum(posix.V.TIME)] = 1;\n   357\n   358        posix.tcsetattr(self.fd, .FLUSH, raw) catch {\n   359            return Error.TerminalSetFailed;\n   360        };\n   361    }\n   362\n   363    /// Exit raw mode: restore original terminal settings.\n   364    fn exitRawMode(self: *Backend) void {\n   365        if (self.original_termios) |original| {\n   366            posix.tcsetattr(self.fd, .FLUSH, original) catch {};\n   367        }\n   368    }\n   369\n   370    /// Enable mouse reporting (SGR mode for better coordinate handling).\n   371    fn enableMouse(self: *Backend) void {\n   372        self.writeEscape(ENABLE_MOUSE_CAPTURE);\n   373        self.writeEscape(ENABLE_MOUSE_SGR);\n   374    }\n   375\n   376    /// Disable mouse reporting.\n   377    fn disableMouse(self: *Backend) void {\n   378        self.writeEscape(DISABLE_MOUSE_SGR);\n   379        self.writeEscape(DISABLE_MOUSE_CAPTURE);\n   380    }\n   381\n   382    /// Write an escape sequence to the terminal.\n   383    fn writeEscape(self: *Backend, seq: []const u8) void {\n   384        const file = std.fs.File{ .handle = self.fd };\n   385        file.writeAll(seq) catch {};\n   386    }\n   387\n   388    /// Flush output to terminal.\n   389    pub fn flush(self: *Backend) void {\n   390        const file = std.fs.File{ .handle = self.fd };\n   391        file.sync() catch {};\n   392    }\n   393\n   394    /// Write bytes to the terminal.\n   395    pub fn write(self: *Backend, data: []const u8) Error!void {\n   396        const file = std.fs.File{ .handle = self.fd };\n   397        file.writeAll(data) catch {\n   398            return Error.IoError;\n   399        };\n   400    }\n   401\n   402    /// Move cursor to home position (0, 0).\n   403    pub fn cursorHome(self: *Backend) void {\n   404        self.writeEscape(CURSOR_HOME);\n   405    }\n   406\n   407    /// Move cursor to specific position (0-indexed).\n   408    pub fn cursorTo(self: *Backend, x: u16, y: u16) void {\n   409        var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n   410        const seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \"\\x1b[{d};{d}H\", .{ y + 1, x + 1 }) catch return;\n   411        self.writeEscape(seq);\n   412    }\n   413\n   414    /// Clear the entire screen.\n   415    pub fn clearScreen(self: *Backend) void {\n   416        self.writeEscape(CLEAR_SCREEN);\n   417    }\n   418\n   419    /// Get terminal size (width, height).\n   420    pub fn getSize(self: *Backend) TerminalSize {\n   421        return getSizeForFd(self.fd);\n   422    }\n   423\n   424    /// Detect terminal color support level.\n   425    /// Checks environment variables COLORTERM and TERM to determine capability.\n   426    /// Returns the highest detected color support level.\n   427    pub fn getColorSupport(_: *Backend) ColorSupport {\n   428        return detectColorSupport();\n   429    }\n   430\n   431    // ANSI escape sequences\n   432    const ENTER_ALTERNATE_SCREEN = \"\\x1b[?1049h\";\n   433    const LEAVE_ALTERNATE_SCREEN = \"\\x1b[?1049l\";\n   434    const HIDE_CURSOR = \"\\x1b[?25l\";\n   435    const SHOW_CURSOR = \"\\x1b[?25h\";\n   436    const CLEAR_SCREEN = \"\\x1b[2J\";\n   437    const CURSOR_HOME = \"\\x1b[H\";\n   438\n   439    const ENABLE_MOUSE_CAPTURE = \"\\x1b[?1000h\\x1b[?1002h\\x1b[?1003h\";\n   440    const DISABLE_MOUSE_CAPTURE = \"\\x1b[?1003l\\x1b[?1002l\\x1b[?1000l\";\n   441    const ENABLE_MOUSE_SGR = \"\\x1b[?1006h\";\n   442    const DISABLE_MOUSE_SGR = \"\\x1b[?1006l\";\n   443\n   444    const ENABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE = \"\\x1b[?2004h\";\n   445    const DISABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE = \"\\x1b[?2004l\";\n   446};\n   447\n   448/// Detect terminal color support from environment variables.\n   449/// This is a standalone function that doesn't require a Backend instance.\n   450/// Checks COLORTERM and TERM environment variables to determine capability.\n   451pub fn detectColorSupport() ColorSupport {\n   452    // Check COLORTERM first - most reliable indicator of true color\n   453    if (std.posix.getenv(\"COLORTERM\")) |colorterm| {\n   454        if (std.mem.eql(u8, colorterm, \"truecolor\") or std.mem.eql(u8, colorterm, \"24bit\")) {\n   455            return .true_color;\n   456        }\n   457    }\n   458\n   459    // Check TERM for terminal type hints\n   460    if (std.posix.getenv(\"TERM\")) |term| {\n   461        // True color indicators in TERM\n   462        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"truecolor\") != null or\n   463            std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"24bit\") != null or\n   464            std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"direct\") != null)\n   465        {\n   466            return .true_color;\n   467        }\n   468\n   469        // 256 color indicators\n   470        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"256color\") != null or\n   471            std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"256\") != null)\n   472        {\n   473            return .extended;\n   474        }\n   475\n   476        // Known modern terminals that support true color\n   477        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"xterm\") or\n   478            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"screen\") or\n   479            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"tmux\") or\n   480            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"vte\") or\n   481            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"gnome\") or\n   482            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"konsole\") or\n   483            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"alacritty\") or\n   484            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"kitty\") or\n   485            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"iterm\"))\n   486        {\n   487            // These terminals typically support at least 256 colors\n   488            // Many support true color but we're conservative\n   489            return .extended;\n   490        }\n   491    }\n   492\n   493    // Default to basic 16-color support\n   494    return .basic;\n   495}\n   496\n   497/// Internal: get terminal size for a specific file descriptor.\n   498fn getSizeForFd(fd: posix.fd_t) TerminalSize {\n   499    var ws: posix.winsize = undefined;\n   500    const result = posix.system.ioctl(fd, posix.T.IOCGWINSZ, @intFromPtr(&ws));\n   501    if (result == 0) {\n   502        return .{ .width = ws.col, .height = ws.row };\n   503    }\n   504    return .{ .width = 80, .height = 24 };\n   505}\n   506\n   507/// Get terminal size without requiring a Backend instance.\n   508/// Useful for initial configuration before Backend initialization.\n   509/// Returns default 80x24 if size cannot be determined.\n   510pub fn getTerminalSize() TerminalSize {\n   511    return getSizeForFd(posix.STDOUT_FILENO);\n   512}\n   513\n   514// ============================================================\n   515// SANITY TESTS - Backend configuration\n   516// ?BackendConfig = null;\n\n/// Perform emergency terminal cleanup.\n/// Called from panic handler and signal handlers.\n/// Writes cleanup sequences directly to fd without checking state,\n/// as the Backend state may be corrupted during panic.\nfn emergencyCleanup() void {\n    const fd = posix.STDOUT_FILENO;\n    const file = std.fs.File{ .handle = fd };\n\n    // Restore terminal based on saved config\n    if (emergency_config) |config| {\n        if (config.bracketed_paste) {\n            file.writeAll(\"\\x1b[?2004l\") catch {};\n        }\n        if (config.mouse_capture) {\n            file.writeAll(\"\\x1b[?1006l\") catch {};\n            file.writeAll(\"\\x1b[?1003l\\x1b[?1002l\\x1b[?1000l\") catch {};\n        }\n        if (config.hide_cursor) {\n emergencyCleanup();\n\n        // Use standard panic behavior\n        _ = ret_addr;\n        std.debug.lockStdErr();\n        const stderr = std.io.getStdErr();\n        stderr.writeAll(msg) catch {};\n        stderr.writeAll(\"\\n\") catch {};\n        @trap();\n    }\n\n    pub fn sentinelMismatch(expected: anytype, found: @TypeOf(expected)) noreturn {\n        _ = found;\n }\n\n    pub fn invalidEnumCast(value: anytype) noreturn {\n        _ = value;\n        call(\"invalid enum cast\", null);\n    }\n\n    pub fn noReturn() noreturn {\n        call(\"noreturn function returned\", null);\n    }\n};\n\n/// Color support levels detected from terminal capabilities.\npub const ColorSupport = enum {\n    /// Basic 8/16 colors (standard ANSI).\n    basic,\n    /// 256 color palette (xterm-256color).\n    extended,\n    /// 24-bit true color (RGB).\n    true_color,\n\n    /// Returns the number of colors supported.\n    pub fn colorCount(self: ColorSupport) u32 {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .basic => 16,\n            .extended => 256,\n            .true_color => 16_777_216,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Returns true if this support level includes TerminalQueryFailed,\n        TerminalSetFailed,\n        IoError,\n    };\n\n    /// Initialize the terminal backend.\n    /// Enables raw mode and optional features based on config.\n    /// fd = posix.STDOUT_FILENO;\n\n        if (!posix.isatty(fd)) {\n            return Error.NotATty;\n        }\n\n        var self = Backend{\n            .fd = fd,\n            .original_termios = null,\n            .config = config,\n            .active = false,\n        };\n\n        try self.enterRawMode();\n        self.active = true;\n\n        // Store state for emergency cleanup\n self.writeEscape(ENTER_ALTERNATE_SCREEN);\n        }\n\n        if (config.hide_cursor) {\n            self.writeEscape(HIDE_CURSOR);\n        }\n\n        if (config.mouse_capture) {\n            self.enableMouse();\n        }\n\n        if (config.bracketed_paste) {\n            self.writeEscape(ENABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE);\n        }\n\n        return self;\n    }\n\n    /// Restore terminal to original state.\n    /// Disables bracketed paste, mouse capture, shows cursor, leaves alternate screen,\n    /// and restores raw mode settings.\n    /// Safe to call multiple times.\n    pub fn deinit(self: *Backend) void {\n        if (!self.active) return;\n\n        // Disable bracketed paste\n        if (self.config.bracketed_paste) {\n            self.writeEscape(DISABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE);\n        }\n\n        // Disable mouse capture\n        if (self.config.mouse_capture) {\n            self.disableMouse();\n        }\n\n        // Show cursor\n        if (self.config.hide_cursor) {\n            self.writeEscape(SHOW_CURSOR);\n        }\n\n        // Leave alternate screen\n        if (self.config.alternate_screen) {\n            self.writeEscape(LEAVE_ALTERNATE_SCREEN);\n        }\n\n        // Restore raw mode (disable raw mode)\n        self.exitRawMode();\n        self.active = false;\n\n        // Clear global state for panic handler\n        if (global_backend == self) {\n            global_backend = null;\n            emergency_original_termios = null;\n            emergency_config = null;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Enter raw mode: disable line buffering, echo, and canonical mode.\n    fn enterRawMode(self: *Backend) Error!void {\n        const original = posix.tcgetattr(self.fd) catch {\n            return Error.TerminalQueryFailed;\n        };\n        self.original_termios = original;\n\n        var raw = original;\n\n        // Input flags: disable break handling, CR-to-NL, parity, strip, flow control\n        raw.iflag.BRKINT = false;\n        raw.iflag.ICRNL = false;\n        raw.iflag.INPCK = false;\n        raw.iflag.ISTRIP = false;\n        raw.iflag.IXON = false;\n\n        // Output flags: disable post-processing\n        raw.oflag.OPOST = false;\n\n        // Control flags: set character size to 8 bits\n        raw.cflag.CSIZE = .CS8;\n\n        // Local flags: disable echo, canonical mode, signals, extended input\n        raw.lflag.ECHO = false;\n        raw.lflag.ICANON = false;\n        raw.lflag.ISIG = false;\n        raw.lflag.IEXTEN = false;\n\n        // Set minimum chars for non-canonical read\n        raw.cc[@intFromEnum(posix.V.MIN)] = 0;\n        raw.cc[@intFromEnum(posix.V.TIME)] = 1;\n\n        posix.tcsetattr(self.fd, .FLUSH, raw) catch {\n            return Error.TerminalSetFailed;\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Exit raw mode: restore original terminal settings.\n    fn exitRawMode(self: *Backend) void {\n        if (self.original_termios) |original| {\n            posix.tcsetattr(self.fd, .FLUSH, original) catch {};\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Enable mouse reporting (SGR mode for better coordinate handling).\n    fn enableMouse(self: *Backend) void {\n        self.writeEscape(ENABLE_MOUSE_CAPTURE);\n        self.writeEscape(ENABLE_MOUSE_SGR);\n    }\n\n    /// Disable mouse reporting.\n    fn disableMouse(self: *Backend) void {\n       const file = std.fs.File{ .handle = self.fd };\n        file.sync() catch {};\n    }\n\n    /// Write bytes to the terminal.\n    pub fn write(self: *Backend, data: []const u8) Error!void {\n        const file = std.fs.File{ .handle = self.fd };\n        file.writeAll(data) catch {\n            return Error.IoError;\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Move cursor to home position (0, 0).\n    pub Checks COLORTERM and TERM environment variables to determine capability.\npub fn detectColorSupport() ColorSupport {\n    // Check COLORTERM first - most reliable indicator of true color\n    if (std.posix.getenv(\"COLORTERM\")) |colorterm| {\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, colorterm, \"truecolor\") or std.mem.eql(u8, colorterm, \"24bit\")) {\n            return .true_color;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Check TERM for terminal type hints\n    if (std.posix.getenv(\"TERM\")) |term| {\n        // True color indicators in TERM\n        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"truecolor\") != null or\n            std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"24bit\") != null or\n            std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"direct\") != null)\n        {\n            return .true_color;\n        }\n\n        // 256 color indicators\n        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"256color\") != null or\n            std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"256\") != null)\n        {\n            return .extended;\n        }\n\n        // Known modern terminals that support true color\n        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"xterm\") or\n            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"screen\") or\n            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"tmux\") or\n            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"vte\") or\n            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"gnome\") or\n            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"konsole\") or\n            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"alacritty\") or\n            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"kitty\") or\n            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"iterm\"))\n        {\n            // These terminals typically support at least 256 colors\n            // Many support true color but we're conservative\n            return .extended;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Default to basic 16-color support\n    return .basic;\n}\n\n/// Internal: get terminal size for a specific file descriptor.\nfn getSizeForFd(fd: posix.fd_t) TerminalSize {\n    var ws: posix.winsize = undefined;\n    const result = posix.system.ioctl(fd, posix.T.IOCGWINSZ, @intFromPtr(&ws));\n    if (result == 0) {\n        return .{ .width = ws.col, .height = ws.row };\n    }\n    return .{ .width = 80, .height = 24 for update and view.\n///\n/// Fields:\n/// - state: Instance of the user's State type\n/// - update_fn: Function pointer for handling events, returns an Action\n/// - view_fn: Function pointer for /// Signature: fn(*State, Event) Action\n        update_fn: *const fn (*State, Event) Action,\n\n        /// View function: receives state and frame, renders the UI.\n        /// Signature: fn(*State,       .mouse_capture = config.mouse_capture,\n                .paste_bracket = config.paste_bracket,\n                .alternate_screen = config.alternate_screen,\n            };\n        }\n\n        /// Returns a BackendConfig derived from this App's configuration.\n        /// Used by the event loop to initialize the terminal backend.\n        pub fn backendConfig(self: Self) frame.\n        /// The view function should use frame.render() to draw widgets.\n        pub fn view(self: *Self, frame: *Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets)) void {\n            self.view_fn(&self.state, Repeat\n        pub fn run(self: *Self, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) RunError!void {\n            // Initialize terminal backend\n            var backend = Backend.init(self.backendConfig()) catch |err| {\n                return switch (err) {\n                    error.NotATty => RunError.NotATty,\n                    error.TerminalQueryFailed => RunError.TerminalQueryFailed,\n                    error.TerminalSetFailed => RunError.TerminalSetFailed,\n                    error.IoError => RunError.IoError,\n                };\n            };\n            defer backend.deinit();\n\n            // Initialize input parser\n            var input = Input.init();\n\n            // Get initial terminal size\n            const initial_size = backend.getSize();\n\n            // Create double buffers for diffing\n            var current_buf = Buffer.init(allocator, initial_size.width, initial_size.height) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer current_buf.deinit();\n\n            var previous_buf = Buffer.init(allocator, initial_size.width, initial_size.height) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer previous_buf.deinit();\n\n            // Allocate update buffer for diff results\n            const max_updates = @as(usize, initial_size.width) * @as(usize, initial_size.height);\n            var updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, max_updates) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer allocator.free(updates);\n\n            // Calculate tick timeout in nanoseconds (0 means no timeout/poll mode)\n            const tick_timeout_ns: ?u64 = if (self.tick_rate_ms > 0)\n                @as(u64, self.tick_rate_ms) * std.time.ns_per_ms\n            else\n                null;\n\n            // Track last tick time for tick events\n            var last_tick: i128 = std.time.nanoTimestamp();\n\n            // Clear screen initially\n            backend.clearScreen();\n            backend.cursorHome();\n\n            // Initial render\n            {\n                current_buf.clear();\n                var frame = Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets).init(&current_buf);\n                self.view(&frame);\n                try renderBuffer(&backend, &current_buf, &previous_buf, updates);\n                @memcpy(previous_buf.cells, current_buf.cells);\n            }\n\n            // Main event loop\n            while (true) {\n                // Poll for events or wait for tick timeout\n                const maybe_event = try pollEvent(&input, &backend, tick_timeout_ns);\n\n                // Handle tick event generation\n                var event: Event = undefined;\n                if (maybe_event) |e| {\n                    event = e;\n                } else if (tick_timeout_ns != null) {\n                    const now = std.time.nanoTimestamp();\n                    if (now - last_tick >= @as(i128, tick_timeout_ns.?)) {\n                        event = Event{ .tick = {} };\n                        last_tick = now;\n                    } else {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                // Handle resize events specially - resize buffers\n                if (event == .resize) {\n                    const new_size = event.resize;\n                    const new_max_updates = @as(usize, new_size.width) * @as(usize, new_size.height);\n\n                    current_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n                    previous_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n\n                    allocator.free(updates);\n                    updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, new_max_updates) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n\n                    // Clear screen on resize\n                    backend.clearScreen();\n                    backend.cursorHome();\n                }\n\n                // Call update function\n                const action = self.update(event);\n\n                // Check for quit action\n                if (action.isQuit()) {\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                // TODO: Handle command actions in the future\n\n                // Clear current buffer and call view function\n                current_buf.clear();\n                var frame = Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets).init(&current_buf);\n                self.view(&frame);\n\n                // Render changes to terminal\n                try renderBuffer(&backend, &current_buf, &previous_buf, updates);\n\n                // Swap buffers (copy current to previous for next diff)\n                @memcpy(previous_buf.cells, current_buf.cells);\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// Poll for an input event from the terminal.\n        /// Returns null if no event is available within the timeout.\n        fn pollEvent(input: *Input, backend: *Backend, timeout_ns: ?u64) RunError!?Event {\n            _ = timeout_ns; // TODO: Implement proper polling with timeout\n\n            // Read available input bytes\n            var buf: [256]u8 = undefined;\n            const bytes_read = std.posix.read(std.posix.STDIN_FILENO, &buf) catch |err| {\n                switch (err) {\n                    error.WouldBlock => return null,\n                    else => return RunError.IoError,\n                }\n            };\n\n            if (bytes_read == 0) {\n                return null;\n            }\n\n            // Parse input bytes into events\n            if (input.parse(buf[0..bytes_read])) |parsed_event| {\n                _ = backend; // Backend used for future resize detection\n                return parsed_event;\n            }\n\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        /// Render buffer changes to the terminal.\n        fn renderBuffer(\n            backend: *Backend,\n            current: *Buffer,\n            previous: *Buffer,\n            update_buffer: []buffer_mod.CellUpdate,\n        ) RunError!void {\n            const changes = current.diff(previous.*, update_buffer);\n\n            if (changes.len == 0) {\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // Build output string with cursor movements and cell contents\n            var output_buf: [8192]u8 = undefined;\n            var output_len: usize = 0;\n\n            var last_x: ?u16 = null;\n            var last_y: ?u16 = null;\n\n            for (changes) |change| {\n                // Move cursor if not consecutive\n                const need_move = if (last_x == null or last_y == null)\n                    true\n                else if (last_y.? != change.y)\n                    true\n                else if (last_x.? + 1 != change.x)\n                    true\n                else\n                    false;\n\n                if (need_move) {\n                    // Add cursor position escape sequence\n                    const move_seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(\n                        output_buf[output_len..],\n                        \"\\x1b[{d};{d}H\",\n                        .{ change.y + 1, change.x + 1 },\n                    ) catch break;\n                    output_len += move_seq.len;\n                }\n\n                // Add style escape sequence\n                const style_seq = renderCellStyle(\n                    output_buf[output_len..],\n                    change.cell,\n                ) catch break;\n                output_len += style_seq.len;\n\n                // Add character\n                if (change.cell.width > 0) {\n                    var char_buf: [4]u8 = undefined;\n                    const char_len = std.unicode.utf8Encode(change.cell.char, &char_buf) catch 1;\n                    if (output_len + char_len <= output_buf.len) {\n                        @memcpy(output_buf[output_len..][0..char_len], char_buf[0..char_len]);\n                        output_len += char_len;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                last_x = change.x;\n                last_y = change.y;\n            }\n\n            // Reset style at the end\n            if (output_len + 4 <= output_buf.len) {\n                @memcpy(output_buf[output_len..][0..4], \"\\x1b[0m\");\n                output_len += 4;\n            }\n\n            // Write to terminal\n            backend.write(output_buf[0..output_len]) catch {\n                return RunError.IoError;\n            };\n            backend.flush();\n        }\n\n        /// Render a cell's style as an ANSI escape sequence.\n        fn renderCellStyle(buf: []u8, cell: cell_mod.Cell) error{NoSpaceLeft}![]u8 {\n            const style = cell.style;\n\n            // Use a fixed-size buffer for building the escape sequence\n            var fbs = std.io.fixedBufferStream(buf);\n            const writer = fbs.writer();\n\n            // Write SGR introducer\n            try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b[0\");\n\n            // Add attributes\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.bold)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";1\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.dim)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";2\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.italic)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";3\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.underline)) {\n                try              try writer.writeAll(\";7\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.strike)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";9\");\n            }\n\n            // Add foreground color if set\n            const fg = style.inner.foreground;\n            if (!fg.eql(@import(\"rich_zig\").Color.default)) {\n                if (fg.color_type == .standard or fg.color_type == .eight_bit) {\n                    if (fg.number) |n| {\n                        if (n < 8) {\n                            try writer.print(\";{d}\", .{30 + n});\n                        } else if (n < 16) {\n                            try writer.print(\";{d}\", .{90 + n - 8});\n                        } else {\n                            try writer.print(\";38;5;{d}\", .{n});\n                        }\n                    }\n                } else if (fg.color_type == .truecolor) {\n                    if (fg.triplet) |t| {\n                        try writer.print(\";38;2;{d};{d};{d}\", .{ t.r, t.g, t.b });\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Add background color if set\n            const bg = style.inner.background;\n            if (!bg.eql(@import(\"rich_zig\").Color.default)) {\n                if (bg.color_type == .standard or bg.color_type == .eight_bit) {\n                    if (bg.number) |n| {\n                        if }\n\n            try writer.writeByte('m');\n\n            return fbs.getWritten();\n        }\n    };\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic framework\n// Generic application type parameterized by user state\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst frame_mod = @import(\"frame.zig\");\nconst event_mod = @import(\"event.zig\");\nconst backend_mod.Backend;\npub const Input = input_mod.Input;\n\n/// App is the main runtime type, generic over the user's state type.\n/// The user provides their own State struct and function pointers for update and view.\n///\n/// Fields:\n/// - state: Instance of the user's State type\n/// - update_fn: Function pointer for handling events, returns an Action\n/// - view_fn: Function pointer for rendering the UI\n/// - tick_rate_ms: Timer interval for tick events (0 = disabled)\n/// - mouse_capture: Enable mouse event reporting\n/// - paste_bracket: Enable bracketed paste mode\n/// - alternate_screen: Use alternate screen buffer\npub fn App(comptime State: type) type {\n    return struct {\n        const Self = @This();\n\n        /// Default max widgets for frame layout cache.\n        pub const DefaultMaxWidgets: usize = 64;\n\n        /// User-defined state instance.\n        state: State,\n\n        /// Update function: receives state and event, returns an Action.\n        /// Signature: fn(*State, Event) Action\n        update_fn: *const fn (*State, Event) Action,\n\n        /// View function: receives state and frame, renders the UI.\n        /// Signature: fn(*State, pointer.\n            view: *const fn (*State, *Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets)) void,\n            /// Timer interval in milliseconds for tick events (0 = disabled).\n            tick_rate_ms: u32 = 0,\n            /// Enable mouse event reporting.\n            mouse_capture: bool = false,\n            /// Enable bracketed paste mode.\n            paste_bracket: bool = false,\n            /// Use alternate screen buffer.\n            alternate_screen: bool = true,\n        };\n\n        /// Initialize an App with the given configuration.\n        pub fn init(config: Config) Self {\n            return .{\n                .state = config.state,\n                .update_fn = config.update,\n                .view_fn = config.view,\n                .tick_rate_ms = config.tick_rate_ms,\n                .mouse_capture = config.mouse_capture,\n                .paste_bracket = config.paste_bracket,\n                .alternate_screen = config.alternate_screen,\n            };\n        }\n\n        /// Returns a BackendConfig derived from this App's configuration.\n        /// Used by the event loop to initialize the terminal backend.\n        pub fn backendConfig(self: Self) @import(\"backend.zig\").BackendConfig {\n            return .{\n                .alternate_screen = self.alternate_screen,\n                .hide_cursor = true,\n                .mouse_capture = self.mouse_capture,\n                .bracketed_paste = self.paste_bracket,\n            };\n        }\n\n        /// Call the update function with an event.\n        /// Returns the action to be processed by the runtime.\n        pub fn update(self: *Self, event: Event) Action {\n            return self.update_fn(&self.state, event);\n        }\n\n        /// Call the view function with a frame.\n        /// The view function should use frame.render() to draw widgets.\n        pub fn view(self: *Self, frame: *Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets)) void {\n            self.view_fn(&self.state, frame);\n        }\n\n        /// Error type for run operations.\n        pub const RunError = error{\n            OutOfMemory,\n            NotATty,\n            TerminalQueryFailed,\n            TerminalSetFailed,\n            IoError,\n        };\n\n        /// Run the main event loop until Action.quit is returned.\n        ///\n        /// Main loop:\n        /// 1. Poll for events (keyboard, mouse, resize, or tick timeout)\n        /// 2. Call update function with the event\n        /// 3. Check action - if .quit, exit loop\n        /// 4. Call view function to describe the UI\n        /// 5. Render by diffing buffers and writing changes to terminal\n        /// 6. Repeat\n        pub fn run(self: *Self, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) RunError!void {\n            // Initialize terminal backend\n            var backend = Backend.init(self.backendConfig()) catch |err| {\n                return switch (err) {\n                    error.NotATty => RunError.NotATty,\n                    error.TerminalQueryFailed => RunError.TerminalQueryFailed,\n                    error.TerminalSetFailed => RunError.TerminalSetFailed,\n                    error.IoError => RunError.IoError,\n                };\n            };\n            defer backend.deinit();\n\n            // Initialize input parser\n            var input = Input.init();\n\n            // Get initial terminal size\n            const initial_size = backend.getSize();\n\n            // Create double buffers for diffing\n            var current_buf = Buffer.init(allocator, initial_size.width, initial_size.height) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer current_buf.deinit();\n\n            var previous_buf = Buffer.init(allocator, initial_size.width, initial_size.height) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer previous_buf.deinit();\n\n            // Allocate update buffer for diff results\n            const max_updates = @as(usize, initial_size.width) * @as(usize, initial_size.height);\n            var updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, max_updates) catch {\n                return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n            };\n            defer allocator.free(updates);\n\n            // Calculate tick timeout in nanoseconds (0 means no timeout/poll mode)\n            const tick_timeout_ns: ?u64 = if (self.tick_rate_ms > 0)\n                @as(u64, self.tick_rate_ms) * std.time.ns_per_ms\n            else\n                null;\n\n            // Track last tick time for tick events\n            var last_tick: i128 = std.time.nanoTimestamp();\n\n            // Clear screen initially\n            backend.clearScreen();\n            backend.cursorHome();\n\n            // Initial render\n            {\n                current_buf.clear();\n                var frame = Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets).init(&current_buf);\n                self.view(&frame);\n                try renderBuffer(&backend, &current_buf, &previous_buf, updates);\n                @memcpy(previous_buf.cells, current_buf.cells);\n            }\n\n            // Main event loop\n            while (true) {\n                // Poll for events or wait for tick timeout\n                const maybe_event = try pollEvent(&input, &backend, tick_timeout_ns);\n\n                // Handle tick event generation\n                var event: Event = undefined;\n                if (maybe_event) |e| {\n                    event = e;\n                } else if (tick_timeout_ns != null) {\n                    const now = std.time.nanoTimestamp();\n                    if (now - last_tick >= @as(i128, tick_timeout_ns.?)) {\n                        event = Event{ .tick = {} };\n                        last_tick = now;\n                    } else {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                // Handle resize events specially - resize buffers\n                if (event == .resize) {\n                    const new_size = event.resize;\n                    const new_max_updates = @as(usize, new_size.width) * @as(usize, new_size.height);\n\n                    current_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n                    previous_buf.resize(new_size.width, new_size.height) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n\n                    allocator.free(updates);\n                    updates = allocator.alloc(buffer_mod.CellUpdate, new_max_updates) catch {\n                        return RunError.OutOfMemory;\n                    };\n\n                    // Clear screen on resize\n                    backend.clearScreen();\n                    backend.cursorHome();\n                }\n\n                // Call update function\n                const action = self.update(event);\n\n                // Check for quit action\n                if (action.isQuit()) {\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                // TODO: Handle command actions in the future\n\n                // Clear current buffer and call view function\n                current_buf.clear();\n                var frame = Frame(DefaultMaxWidgets).init(&current_buf);\n                self.view(&frame);\n\n                // Render changes to terminal\n                try renderBuffer(&backend, &current_buf, &previous_buf, updates);\n\n                // Swap buffers (copy current to previous for next diff)\n                @memcpy(previous_buf.cells, current_buf.cells);\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// Poll for an input event from the terminal.\n        /// Returns null if no event is available within the timeout.\n        fn pollEvent(input: *Input, backend: *Backend, timeout_ns: ?u64) RunError!?Event {\n            _ = timeout_ns; // TODO: Implement proper polling with timeout\n\n            // Read available input bytes\n            var buf: [256]u8 = undefined;\n            const bytes_read = std.posix.read(std.posix.STDIN_FILENO, &buf) catch |err| {\n                switch (err) {\n                    error.WouldBlock => return null,\n                    else => return RunError.IoError,\n                }\n            };\n\n            if (bytes_read == 0) {\n                return null;\n            }\n\n            // Parse input bytes into events\n            if (input.parse(buf[0..bytes_read])) |parsed_event| {\n                _ = backend; // Backend used for future resize detection\n                return parsed_event;\n            }\n\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        /// Render buffer changes to the terminal.\n        fn renderBuffer(\n            backend: *Backend,\n            current: *Buffer,\n            previous: *Buffer,\n            update_buffer: []buffer_mod.CellUpdate,\n        ) RunError!void {\n            const changes = current.diff(previous.*, update_buffer);\n\n            if (changes.len == 0) {\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // Build output string with cursor movements and cell contents\n            var output_buf: [8192]u8 = undefined;\n            var output_len: usize = 0;\n\n            var last_x: ?u16 = null;\n            var last_y: ?u16 = null;\n\n            for (changes) |change| {\n                // Move cursor if not consecutive (different row or non-adjacent column)\n                const consecutive = last_x != null and last_y != null and\n                    last_y.? == change.y and last_x.? + 1 == change.x;\n\n                if (!consecutive) {\n                    // Add cursor position escape sequence\n                    const move_seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(\n                        output_buf[output_len..],\n                        \"\\x1b[{d};{d}H\",\n                        .{ change.y + 1, change.x + 1 },\n                    ) catch break;\n                    output_len += move_seq.len;\n                }\n\n                // Add style escape sequence\n                const style_seq = renderCellStyle(\n                    output_buf[output_len..],\n                    change.cell,\n                ) catch break;\n                output_len += style_seq.len;\n\n                // Add character\n                if (change.cell.width > 0) {\n                    var char_buf: [4]u8 = undefined;\n                    const char_len = std.unicode.utf8Encode(change.cell.char, &char_buf) catch 1;\n                    if (output_len + char_len <= output_buf.len) {\n                        @memcpy(output_buf[output_len..][0..char_len], char_buf[0..char_len]);\n                        output_len += char_len;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                last_x = change.x;\n                last_y = change.y;\n            }\n\n            // Reset style at the end\n            if (output_len + 4 <= output_buf.len) {\n                @memcpy(output_buf[output_len..][0..4], \"\\x1b[0m\");\n                output_len += 4;\n            }\n\n            // Write to terminal\n            backend.write(output_buf[0..output_len]) catch {\n                return RunError.IoError;\n            };\n            backend.flush();\n        }\n\n        /// Render a cell's style as an ANSI escape sequence.\n        fn renderCellStyle(buf: []u8, cell: cell_mod.Cell) error{NoSpaceLeft}![]u8 {\n            const style = cell.style;\n\n            // Use a fixed-size buffer for building the escape sequence\n            var fbs = std.io.fixedBufferStream(buf);\n            const writer = fbs.writer();\n\n            // Write SGR introducer\n            try writer.writeAll(\"\\x1b[0\");\n\n            // Add attributes\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.bold)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";1\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.dim)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";2\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.italic)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";3\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.underline)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";4\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.blink)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";5\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.reverse)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";7\");\n            }\n            if (style.hasAttribute(.strike)) {\n                try writer.writeAll(\";9\");\n            }\n\n            // Add foreground color if set\n            const fg = style.inner.foreground;\n            if (!fg.eql(@import(\"rich_zig\").Color.default)) {\n                if (fg.color_type == .standard or fg.color_type == .eight_bit) {\n                    if (fg.number) |n| {\n                        if (n < 8) {\n                            try writer.print(\";{d}\", .{30 + n});\n                        } else if (n < 16) {\n                            try writer.print(\";{d}\", .{90 + n - 8});\n }\n\n            // Add background color if set\n            const bg = style.inner.background;\n            if (!bg.eql(@import(\"rich_zig\").Color.default)) {\n                if (bg.color_type == },\n            'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home } },\n            'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end } },\n            'Z' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .backtab } }, // Shift+Tab\n            else => self.parseCsiParams(bytes),\n        };","originalFile":"// Terminal input parsing for zithril TUI framework\n// Parses raw terminal bytes into Event types\n// Handles ANSI escape sequences for keys, mouse, and special characters\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst event_mod = @import(\"event.zig\");\n\npub const Event = event_mod.Event;\npub const Key = event_mod.Key;\npub const KeyCode = event_mod.KeyCode;\npub const Modifiers = event_mod.Modifiers;\npub const Mouse = event_mod.Mouse;\npub const MouseKind = event_mod.MouseKind;\npub const Size = event_mod.Size;\n\n/// Input parser state machine.\n/// Parses raw terminal input bytes into Event types.\npub const Input = struct {\n    /// Buffer for incomplete escape sequences\n    buffer: [32]u8 = undefined,\n    /// Number of bytes in buffer\n    buffer_len: usize = 0,\n    /// Whether we're in a paste sequence\n    in_paste: bool = false,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    /// Initialize a new input parser.\n    pub fn init() Self {\n        return .{};\n    }\n\n    /// Parse input bytes and return an event if one is complete.\n    /// May consume partial input for multi-byte sequences.\n    pub fn parse(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // Handle bracketed paste mode\n        if (self.in_paste) {\n            return self.parsePaste(bytes);\n        }\n\n        // Check for escape sequence\n        if (bytes[0] == 0x1b) {\n            return self.parseEscape(bytes);\n        }\n\n        // Handle control characters\n        if (bytes[0] < 0x20) {\n            return self.parseControl(bytes[0]);\n        }\n\n        // Handle regular UTF-8 character\n        return self.parseUtf8(bytes);\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a control character (0x00-0x1F).\n    fn parseControl(self: *Self, byte: u8) ?Event {\n        _ = self;\n        return switch (byte) {\n            0x00 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = ' ' }, .modifiers = .{ .ctrl = true } } }, // Ctrl+Space\n            0x09 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .tab } }, // Tab\n            0x0a, 0x0d => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .enter } }, // Enter (LF or CR)\n            0x7f => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .backspace } }, // Backspace (DEL)\n            // Ctrl+A through Ctrl+Z (excluding tab=0x09, enter=0x0a, and 0x0d)\n            0x01...0x08, 0x0b, 0x0c, 0x0e...0x1a => |b| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = 'a' + (b - 1) }, .modifiers = .{ .ctrl = true } } },\n            0x1b => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } }, // Escape (handled elsewhere)\n            else => null,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse an escape sequence.\n    fn parseEscape(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        if (bytes.len == 1) {\n            // Just ESC by itself\n            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n        }\n\n        const second = bytes[1];\n\n        // CSI sequence (ESC [)\n        if (second == '[') {\n            return self.parseCsi(bytes[2..]);\n        }\n\n        // SS3 sequence (ESC O)\n        if (second == 'O') {\n            return self.parseSs3(bytes[2..]);\n        }\n\n        // Alt+Escape\n        if (second == 0x1b) {\n            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape, .modifiers = .{ .alt = true } } };\n        }\n\n        // Alt+key (printable ASCII)\n        if (second >= 0x20 and second < 0x7f) {\n            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = second }, .modifiers = .{ .alt = true } } };\n        }\n\n        return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a CSI (Control Sequence Introducer) sequence.\n    /// Format: ESC [ <params> <final>\n    fn parseCsi(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n        }\n\n        // Check for mouse sequences\n        if (bytes[0] == 'M' or bytes[0] == '<') {\n            return self.parseMouse(bytes);\n        }\n\n        // Check for bracketed paste\n        if (bytes.len >= 4 and bytes[0] == '2' and bytes[1] == '0' and bytes[2] == '0' and bytes[3] == '~') {\n            self.in_paste = true;\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // Parse arrow keys and simple sequences\n        if (bytes.len >= 1) {\n            return switch (bytes[0]) {\n                'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up } },\n                'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down } },\n                'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right } },\n                'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left } },\n                'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home } },\n                'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end } },\n                'Z' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .backtab } }, // Shift+Tab\n                else => self.parseCsiParams(bytes),\n            };\n        }\n\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse CSI sequences with parameters.\n    fn parseCsiParams(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        _ = self;\n\n        // Find the final character\n        var i: usize = 0;\n        var param1: u16 = 0;\n        var param2: u16 = 0;\n        var in_second_param = false;\n\n        while (i < bytes.len) : (i += 1) {\n            const c = bytes[i];\n            if (c >= '0' and c <= '9') {\n                if (in_second_param) {\n                    param2 = param2 * 10 + (c - '0');\n                } else {\n                    param1 = param1 * 10 + (c - '0');\n                }\n            } else if (c == ';') {\n                in_second_param = true;\n            } else {\n                // Final character\n                return parseCsiFinal(c, param1, param2);\n            }\n        }\n\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse the final character of a CSI sequence.\n    fn parseCsiFinal(final: u8, param1: u16, param2: u16) ?Event {\n        // Extract modifiers from param2 (CSI 1;2A = Shift+Up, etc.)\n        const mods = modifiersFromParam(param2);\n\n        return switch (final) {\n            'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up, .modifiers = mods } },\n            'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down, .modifiers = mods } },\n            'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right, .modifiers = mods } },\n            'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left, .modifiers = mods } },\n            'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n            'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n            '~' => switch (param1) {\n                1 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n                2 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .insert, .modifiers = mods } },\n                3 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .delete, .modifiers = mods } },\n                4 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n                5 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .page_up, .modifiers = mods } },\n                6 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .page_down, .modifiers = mods } },\n                7 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home, .modifiers = mods } },\n                8 => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end, .modifiers = mods } },\n                11...15 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 10) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F1-F5\n                17...21 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 11) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F6-F10\n                23, 24 => |p| Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = @intCast(p - 12) }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F11-F12\n                200 => null, // Bracketed paste start (handled elsewhere)\n                201 => null, // Bracketed paste end (handled elsewhere)\n                else => null,\n            },\n            'P' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 1 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F1\n            'Q' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 2 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F2\n            'R' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 3 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F3\n            'S' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 4 }, .modifiers = mods } }, // F4\n            else => null,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Convert modifier parameter to Modifiers struct.\n    /// Terminal convention: 1=none, 2=shift, 3=alt, 4=shift+alt, 5=ctrl, etc.\n    fn modifiersFromParam(param: u16) Modifiers {\n        if (param == 0 or param == 1) {\n            return Modifiers{};\n        }\n\n        const p = param - 1;\n        return Modifiers{\n            .shift = (p & 1) != 0,\n            .alt = (p & 2) != 0,\n            .ctrl = (p & 4) != 0,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse an SS3 (Single Shift 3) sequence.\n    /// Used by some terminals for function keys and keypad.\n    fn parseSs3(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        _ = self;\n        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n            return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .escape } };\n        }\n\n        return switch (bytes[0]) {\n            'A' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .up } },\n            'B' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .down } },\n            'C' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .right } },\n            'D' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .left } },\n            'H' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .home } },\n            'F' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .end } },\n            'P' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 1 } } },\n            'Q' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 2 } } },\n            'R' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 3 } } },\n            'S' => Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .f = 4 } } },\n            else => null,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse mouse sequences (X10 or SGR mode).\n    fn parseMouse(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        _ = self;\n\n        if (bytes.len == 0) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // SGR mode: ESC [ < Cb ; Cx ; Cy M/m\n        if (bytes[0] == '<') {\n            return parseMouseSgr(bytes[1..]);\n        }\n\n        // X10 mode: ESC [ M Cb Cx Cy\n        if (bytes[0] == 'M') {\n            return parseMouseX10(bytes[1..]);\n        }\n\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse SGR mouse sequence.\n    /// Format: <Cb;Cx;Cy M or <Cb;Cx;Cy m\n    fn parseMouseSgr(bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        var i: usize = 0;\n        var cb: u16 = 0;\n        var cx: u16 = 0;\n        var cy: u16 = 0;\n        var param_index: u8 = 0;\n\n        while (i < bytes.len) : (i += 1) {\n            const c = bytes[i];\n            if (c >= '0' and c <= '9') {\n                switch (param_index) {\n                    0 => cb = cb * 10 + (c - '0'),\n                    1 => cx = cx * 10 + (c - '0'),\n                    2 => cy = cy * 10 + (c - '0'),\n                    else => {},\n                }\n            } else if (c == ';') {\n                param_index += 1;\n            } else if (c == 'M' or c == 'm') {\n                // M = button press, m = button release\n                const is_release = (c == 'm');\n\n                // Decode button and modifiers from cb\n                const button = @as(u8, @intCast(cb & 0x03));\n                const shift = (cb & 0x04) != 0;\n                const alt = (cb & 0x08) != 0;\n                const ctrl = (cb & 0x10) != 0;\n                const motion = (cb & 0x20) != 0;\n                const wheel = (cb & 0x40) != 0;\n\n                const kind: MouseKind = if (wheel)\n                    if (button == 0) .scroll_up else .scroll_down\n                else if (motion)\n                    .drag\n                else if (is_release)\n                    .up\n                else\n                    .down;\n\n                // SGR coordinates are 1-based\n                const x = if (cx > 0) cx - 1 else 0;\n                const y = if (cy > 0) cy - 1 else 0;\n\n                return Event{\n                    .mouse = .{\n                        .x = x,\n                        .y = y,\n                        .kind = kind,\n                        .modifiers = .{\n                            .shift = shift,\n                            .alt = alt,\n                            .ctrl = ctrl,\n                        },\n                    },\n                };\n            }\n        }\n\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse X10 mouse sequence.\n    /// Format: M Cb Cx Cy (all encoded as Cb+32, Cx+32, Cy+32)\n    fn parseMouseX10(bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        if (bytes.len < 3) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        const cb = bytes[0] -| 32;\n        const cx = bytes[1] -| 32;\n        const cy = bytes[2] -| 32;\n\n        const button = cb & 0x03;\n        const shift = (cb & 0x04) != 0;\n        const alt = (cb & 0x08) != 0;\n        const ctrl = (cb & 0x10) != 0;\n        const motion = (cb & 0x20) != 0;\n        const wheel = (cb & 0x40) != 0;\n\n        const kind: MouseKind = if (wheel)\n            if (button == 0) .scroll_up else .scroll_down\n        else if (motion)\n            .drag\n        else if (button == 3)\n            .up // X10 uses button 3 for release\n        else\n            .down;\n\n        return Event{\n            .mouse = .{\n                .x = cx,\n                .y = cy,\n                .kind = kind,\n                .modifiers = .{\n                    .shift = shift,\n                    .alt = alt,\n                    .ctrl = ctrl,\n                },\n            },\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a paste sequence.\n    fn parsePaste(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        // Look for paste end sequence: ESC [ 2 0 1 ~\n        const end_seq = \"\\x1b[201~\";\n        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, bytes, end_seq)) |_| {\n            self.in_paste = false;\n            // For now, we don't expose paste content as events\n            // Future: could return a paste event with content\n        }\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a UTF-8 character sequence.\n    fn parseUtf8(self: *Self, bytes: []const u8) ?Event {\n        _ = self;\n\n        // Determine UTF-8 sequence length from first byte\n        const len = utf8ByteLen(bytes[0]);\n\n        if (len == 0) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        if (bytes.len < len) {\n            // Incomplete sequence\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // Decode the codepoint\n        const codepoint = std.unicode.utf8Decode(bytes[0..len]) catch {\n            return null;\n        };\n\n        return Event{ .key = .{ .code = .{ .char = codepoint } } };\n    }\n};\n\n/// Get the length of a UTF-8 sequence from its first byte.\nfn utf8ByteLen(byte: u8) usize {\n    if (byte < 0x80) return 1;\n    if (byte < 0xc0) return 0; // Continuation byte\n    if (byte < 0xe0) return 2;\n    if (byte < 0xf0) return 3;\n    if (byte < 0xf8) return 4;\n    return 0;\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic input parsing\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: Input.init creates parser\" {\n    const input = Input.init();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), input.buffer_len);\n    try std.testing.expect(!input.in_paste);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: parse single ASCII character\" {\n    var input = Input.init();\n    const event = input.parse(\"a\");\n    try std.testing.expect(event != null);\n    try std.testing.expect(event.? == .key);\n    try std.testing.expect(event.?.key.code == .char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'a'), event.?.key.code.char);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: parse escape key\" {\n    var input = Input.init();\n    const event = input.parse(\"\\x1b\");\n    try std.testing.expect(event != null);\n    try std.testing.expect(event.?.key.code == .escape);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: parse enter key\" {\n    var input = Input.init();\n    const event = input.parse(\"\\r\");\n    try std.testing.expect(event != null);\n    try std.testing.expect(event.?.key.code == .enter);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: parse tab key\" {\n    var input = Input.init();\n    const event = input.parse(\"\\t\");\n    try std.testing.expect(event != null);\n    try std.testing.expect(event.?.key.code == .tab);\n}\n\n//
